## Pages

### Controlled vocabulary

- [`meaning-senses.md`](meaning-senses.md) — typology of senses of "meaning". Mechanically required by `senselint`.

### Base — concepts

- [`base/concepts/distributional-meaning.md`](base/concepts/distributional-meaning.md) — distributional view; the null hypothesis for constructional-meaning claims. Grounded in Bender & Koller, Piantadosi & Hill, Weissweiler. (filled 2026-05-29)
- [`base/concepts/referential-meaning.md`](base/concepts/referential-meaning.md) — sense/reference/externalist; the LLM-meaning debate's hardest cases. **Deepened 2026-05-31** with a worked internalism-vs-externalism section (Putnam/Burge/Evans externalism vs Chomsky/Fodor narrow content) + the grounding nulls mapped onto the externalist axis (the narrow signal saturates the easy cases; the wide signal stays untested where it would matter) + why the reference-anchor gap is *structural*. Grounded in Bender & Koller; Putnam/Evans/Burge/Chomsky/Fodor characterized (in wanted). (filled 2026-05-29; deepened 2026-05-31)
- [`base/concepts/inferential-meaning.md`](base/concepts/inferential-meaning.md) — conceptual-role / inferential semantics; the strongest pro-LLM-meaning position. **Deepened 2026-05-31**: Brandom's normative (social) inferentialism distinguished from Piantadosi-Hill's internalist conceptual role; what the project's Tier-4 results do/don't show (a thin, NLI-style inferential role, itself instrument-fragile — not Brandom's normative articulation); the relational bridge (the pilot null fits the internalist, not the Brandomian, reading). Grounded in Piantadosi & Hill; Brandom/Sellars characterized (in wanted). (filled 2026-05-29; deepened 2026-05-31)
- [`base/concepts/grounding.md`](base/concepts/grounding.md) — form-vs-meaning (Bender & Koller, binary) vs. grounding-as-gradual (Lyre, three-dimensional); the project's gradient stance. (filled 2026-05-29)
- [`base/concepts/formal-vs-functional-competence.md`](base/concepts/formal-vs-functional-competence.md) — Mahowald et al. 2024 distinction; structural knowledge vs. language-in-the-world. (filled 2026-05-29)
- [`base/concepts/constructional-meaning.md`](base/concepts/constructional-meaning.md) — CxG form–meaning pairing; underwrites the `constructional` tag. Grounded in Weissweiler 2023. (filled 2026-05-29)
- [`base/concepts/coercion.md`](base/concepts/coercion.md) — constructional coercion: the construction overriding the verb (caused-motion, *way*); the sharpest Tier-4 wedge; the project's own add-vs-cancel asymmetry observation. Sharpens `constructional-meaning`; grounds the four argument-structure result pages. (created 2026-05-29)
- [`base/concepts/relational-meaning.md`](base/concepts/relational-meaning.md) — meaning constituted *between* agents (the charter's distinctive, under-explored second axis); the "second ladder" with trajectory-dependence (live-vs-shuffled) as candidate bottom rung. **First in-repo result landed 2026-05-31: a first-class null** ([`result/relational-reference-game-v1`](findings/results/relational-reference-game-v1.md) — order-insensitive conventions; floor characterized, rung not climbed). (created 2026-05-29; updated 2026-05-31)
- [`base/concepts/polysemy.md`](base/concepts/polysemy.md) — polysemy (graded, related senses) vs. homonymy (discrete, unrelated); sense as Fregean `Sinn` at fine grain; the base-concept home for the project's **lexical wedge**. Refines `referential-meaning`; the polysemy/homonymy split is the wedge's built-in internal control; distributional context-similarity is the null. Canonical lexicographic sources (Cruse/Murphy/Lyons) still in `wanted.md`. (created 2026-05-29)
- [`base/concepts/multimodal-compositionality.md`](base/concepts/multimodal-compositionality.md) — the VLM-compositionality question: do vision-language models compose lexical/relational meaning across modalities or behave like *bags-of-words*? The cross-modal analogue of the constructional wedge; a base-layer home for `grounded.perceptual`. Flags that the cited benchmarks are *discriminative* (image-text matching), unlike the project's *generative* panel. Grounded in Winoground + ARO/SugarCrepe. (created 2026-05-30; **multimodal axis**)
- [`base/concepts/symbol-grounding-problem.md`](base/concepts/symbol-grounding-problem.md) — Harnad's symbol-grounding problem: the symbol→sensorimotor *anchoring mechanism* (distinct from `grounding.md`'s binary-vs-gradual debate, which it refines); the philosophical ancestor of Bender-Koller form-vs-meaning. Grounded in Harnad 1990 + Barsalou 1999. (created 2026-05-30; **multimodal axis**)
- [`base/concepts/embodied-cognition.md`](base/concepts/embodied-cognition.md) — sensorimotor/simulation theories of meaning (Barsalou perceptual symbols) and **where they make testable contact with model behaviour** (honest about what is *not* testable on a VLM); carries the still-unanchored `referential.externalist` (Putnam/Evans) gap as embodiment's philosophical cousin. (created 2026-05-30; **multimodal axis**)
- [`base/concepts/truth-conditional-and-use-meaning.md`](base/concepts/truth-conditional-and-use-meaning.md) — truth-conditional/model-theoretic semantics (Frege→Tarski→Davidson→Montague) vs. meaning-as-use (Wittgenstein: language-games, family resemblance); argues the project's behavioral-probing method is methodologically a *use*-theoretic bet. Maps the lexical gradience positive (use/family-resemblance) + the polysemy/homonymy powered null (strains discrete senses; **silent** on the strongest truth-conditional claim); truth-conditional LLM meaning is the un-probed cell (no in-repo reference anchor). (created 2026-05-31; **theory session**)
- [`base/concepts/compositionality.md`](base/concepts/compositionality.md) — the Fregean principle of compositionality + the Construction-Grammar reframing (constructions as meaning-bearing parts; coercion as the limiting case). Maps CC multi-step composition (neg×neg=pos beats a single-clause heuristic), caused-motion/way (construction contributes what the verb cannot), the coercion bridge (partial de-confounding), and the VLM bag-of-words *failure* (Winoground/ARO; discriminative-vs-generative caveat). (created 2026-05-31; **theory session**)
- [`base/concepts/frame-and-prototype-semantics.md`](base/concepts/frame-and-prototype-semantics.md) — Fillmore frame semantics (the semantic backbone of CxG) + Rosch/Lakoff prototype/graded-category structure. Maps the lexical gradience positive (graded, prototype-*consistent* behavior — not asserted as prototype *representation*) + the polysemy/homonymy null (consistent with radial structure; silent on discreteness). (created 2026-05-31; **theory session**)
- [`base/concepts/semantic-holism.md`](base/concepts/semantic-holism.md) — atomism↔molecularism↔holism + the holism objection (Fodor & Lepore) to conceptual-role semantics, and why it bites for LLMs (distributional models are holistic; Piantadosi & Hill's pro-LLM account is explicitly holist). Maps the cross-axis dissociation (mild n=3 strain on "one entangled content store") + cross-model relational convergence (flagged interpretation, not a holism test). (created 2026-05-31; **theory session**)
- [`base/concepts/deflationary-and-eliminativist-llm-meaning.md`](base/concepts/deflationary-and-eliminativist-llm-meaning.md) — the eliminativist ("stochastic parrots"; Bender-Koller form-only) → deflationary ("just distributional") → the project's descriptivist ("describe, don't litigate"; Lyre gradualism) spectrum. Maps which findings bear toward deflation (the relational null + two grounding nulls) vs. strain strict eliminativism (the gradience positive; CC composition); argues behavioral evidence never *refutes* deflationism. (created 2026-05-31; **theory session**)

### Base — sources

- [`base/sources/bender-koller-2020-climbing.md`](base/sources/bender-koller-2020-climbing.md) — Bender & Koller 2020, ACL; form-vs-meaning argument, octopus thought experiment; grounds `grounded` tag. **status: received** (page-level quotes extracted 2026-05-28).
- [`base/sources/bender-2021-stochastic-parrots.md`](base/sources/bender-2021-stochastic-parrots.md) — Bender, Gebru, McMillan-Major & Shmitchell 2021, FAccT '21 (pp. 610–623; DOI 10.1145/3442188.3445922; CC BY 4.0); the **origin of the "stochastic parrot" slogan** — the eliminativist/deflationary foil [`concept/deflationary-and-eliminativist-llm-meaning`](base/concepts/deflationary-and-eliminativist-llm-meaning.md) maps. §6.1 gives the now-canonical form-without-meaning definition verbatim ("a system for haphazardly stitching together sequences of linguistic forms … without any reference to meaning"), the "coherence is in the eye of the beholder" projected-meaning point, and "not grounded in communicative intent". Pairs with [`source/bender-koller-2020-climbing`](base/sources/bender-koller-2020-climbing.md) (shared author): cite Bender & Koller for the *argument*, this for the *slogan*. **Map/foil, not a human anchor** (a critical position paper; no experiments/annotations — cannot ground any empirical claim). Upgrades the concept page's prior "(not in-repo; characterization)" flag to a sourced verbatim quote. **status: received** (6 §6.1/§2 quotes verified character-for-character from the CC BY 4.0 PDF via pdfminer, section-level locators, 2026-06-15). (**philosophical track**)
- [`base/sources/lyre-2024-semantic-grounding.md`](base/sources/lyre-2024-semantic-grounding.md) — Lyre 2024, arXiv 2402.10992; grounding-as-gradual, three-dimensional typology (functional/social/causal); grounds `grounded` sub-tags. **status: received** (page-level quotes extracted 2026-05-28).
- [`base/sources/piantadosi-hill-2022-meaning-without-reference.md`](base/sources/piantadosi-hill-2022-meaning-without-reference.md) — Piantadosi & Hill 2022, arXiv 2208.02957; conceptual-role semantics, meaning without reference; grounds `inferential` tag. **status: received** (section-level quotes extracted 2026-05-28).
- [`base/sources/weissweiler-2023-cxg-insight.md`](base/sources/weissweiler-2023-cxg-insight.md) — Weissweiler et al. 2023, GURT; CxG-probing methodology, form–meaning pairing as test criterion; grounds `constructional` tag. **status: received** (section-level quotes extracted 2026-05-28).
- [`base/sources/weissweiler-2022-comparative-correlative.md`](base/sources/weissweiler-2022-comparative-correlative.md) — Weissweiler, Hofmann, Köksal & Schütze 2022, EMNLP; probes BERT/RoBERTa/DeBERTa on the English comparative correlative and finds they **recognise the structure but fail to use its meaning** — a syntax-vs-semantics dissociation. The single-construction empirical precedent the 2023 survey generalizes; the CC is also one of Scivetti 2025's 8 constructions. **status: received** (abstract verbatim from ACL Anthology + 3 section-level body quotes from ar5iv HTML, 2026-05-29).
- [`base/sources/scivetti-2025-beyond-memorization.md`](base/sources/scivetti-2025-beyond-memorization.md) — Scivetti, Tayyar Madabushi et al. 2025, IJCNLP-AACL; CxG inference benchmark over 8 phrasal constructions (incl. caused-motion, conative, way-manner) with human comparison; GPT-o1 drops >40% on syntactically-identical/semantically-divergent forms. Resolves both P2 wants. **status: received** (abstract verbatim from ACL Anthology + 3 section-level body quotes from arXiv v1 HTML, 2026-05-29).
- [`base/sources/mahowald-2024-dissociating.md`](base/sources/mahowald-2024-dissociating.md) — Mahowald et al. 2024, TiCS 28(6); formal-vs-functional competence distinction, neuroscience grounding; primary reference for `functional-vs-formal` tag. **status: received** (section-level quotes extracted 2026-05-28).
- [`base/sources/mahowald-2023-aann-judgments.md`](base/sources/mahowald-2023-aann-judgments.md) — Mahowald 2023, EACL (arXiv 2301.12564); GPT-3 (text-davinci-002) rates the AANN construction; broadly human-like on form, with the author's own caveat that this is "not the same thing as showing that it understands the meaning or function." The argument/findings record (the dataset is the separate stimuli resource); grounds [`claim/formal-competence-aann-ceiling`](findings/claims/formal-competence-aann-ceiling.md). **status: received** (abstract + 3 section-level body quotes verbatim, 2026-05-29).
- [`base/sources/thrush-2022-winoground.md`](base/sources/thrush-2022-winoground.md) — Thrush et al. 2022, CVPR; **Winoground**, a human-curated visio-linguistic compositionality benchmark (image-caption pairs differing only in word order); SOTA VLMs near/below chance → non-compositional. **status: received** (abstract verbatim from arXiv 2204.03162; §3.1 curation + Table-3 random/human figures re-verified verbatim against ar5iv HTML 2026-05-31; no inter-annotator-agreement statistic exists — confirmed; page-level CVPR PDF provenance still pending). (**multimodal axis**)
- [`base/sources/yuksekgonul-2023-aro.md`](base/sources/yuksekgonul-2023-aro.md) — Yuksekgonul et al. 2023, ICLR; **ARO** ("bags-of-words") — VLMs insensitive to word order/attribute-binding; includes a **SugarCrepe** (Hsieh et al. 2023, NeurIPS) abstract note on benchmark text-only artefacts. **status: received** (abstracts + §2.3 body figures verbatim, re-verified against ar5iv HTML 2026-05-31; the per-model scores live in Figure 1 / appendix — *not* Table 1, which lists perturbations — and those numeric cells remain unverified; dedicated SugarCrepe page `wanted`). (**multimodal axis**)
- [`base/sources/harnad-1990-symbol-grounding.md`](base/sources/harnad-1990-symbol-grounding.md) — Harnad 1990, *Physica D* 42:335–346; the **symbol-grounding problem** + the Chinese/Chinese dictionary-go-round; grounding requires connection to sensorimotor categories. The ancestor of the form-vs-meaning line. **status: received** (abstract + key passages verbatim from arXiv cs/9906002 self-archive — re-verified 2026-05-31, three previously-approximate body quotes corrected to exact text; journal pagination still pending the paywalled/scanned Physica D PDF). (**multimodal axis**)
- [`base/sources/barsalou-1999-perceptual-symbol-systems.md`](base/sources/barsalou-1999-perceptual-symbol-systems.md) — Barsalou 1999, *BBS* 22:577–660; **perceptual symbol systems** — concepts as modal perceptual simulations; backbone for `grounded.perceptual`. **status: received** (abstract verbatim from Cambridge Core, 2026-05-30; some body quotes secondary-source/approximate, flagged in-page, pending PDF). (**multimodal axis**)
- [`base/sources/ashery-2025-llm-conventions.md`](base/sources/ashery-2025-llm-conventions.md) — Ashery, Aiello & Baronchelli 2025, *Science Advances* 11(20); naming-game convention emergence in LLM populations (collective bias, committed-minority tipping points) — the **first dedicated `relational`-axis source** (foil, not anchor: shows coordination/convergence with **no trajectory-dependence control and no human baseline** — exactly the gap the project's pilot fills). Records the live Barrie & Törnberg data-leakage critique + authors' reply as a calibration caveat. **status: received** (section-level quotes verified against arXiv HTML v2, 2026-06-12). (**relational axis**)
- [`base/sources/imai-2025-vlm-common-ground.md`](base/sources/imai-2025-vlm-common-ground.md) — Imai, İnan, Sicilia & Alikhani 2025, arXiv 2509.03805; VLM self-play dyads vs 2,506 human dialogues in the PhotoBook reference game — the **conceptual-pacts/entrainment question asked of model dyads directly**; qualitatively corroborates the pilot's "convergence without human-like compression" pattern (its "grounding" is Clark-style conversational grounding, not Harnad symbol grounding; no order-scramble control). **status: received** (section-level quotes verified against arXiv HTML v1, 2026-06-12). (**relational axis**)
- [`base/sources/schuele-2025-semantics-of-llms.md`](base/sources/schuele-2025-semantics-of-llms.md) — Schuele 2025 (arXiv 2507.05448; orig. *Intellectica* 81:15–36, 2024), "On the Semantics of Large Language Models"; applies the Frege/Russell apparatus to LLM internals and lands on a **split verdict**: meaningless on a reference-only theory, but the latent space "shares certain properties with Frege's notion of sense" — the first in-repo published argument for the **sense-without-reference** reading, triangulating Bender–Koller (engaged by name) and Piantadosi–Hill (cited approvingly). Conceptual analysis only; grounds framing, no empirical claims. **status: received** (abstract + 7 section-level quotes verbatim-verified against arXiv HTML v1, 2026-06-12). (**philosophical track**)
- [`base/sources/milliere-buckner-2024-philosophical-intro-i.md`](base/sources/milliere-buckner-2024-philosophical-intro-i.md) — Millière & Buckner 2024, arXiv 2401.03910 (Part I of the two-part philosophical survey); maps the classic debates (form-vs-meaning, symbol grounding, stochastic-parrots deflationism, compositionality, reference, world models) onto LLMs and argues most are *empirically underdetermined* rather than settled — the strongest in-repo survey backbone for the philosophical track; grounds the grounding / symbol-grounding / deflationary / compositionality / inferential / referential concept pages; no empirical claims of its own. Part II (arXiv 2405.03207) now catalogued (next entry). **status: received** (abstract + 7 section-level quotes verbatim-verified against the ar5iv rendering of v1, 2026-06-13). (**philosophical track**)
- [`base/sources/milliere-buckner-2024-philosophical-intro-ii.md`](base/sources/milliere-buckner-2024-philosophical-intro-ii.md) — Millière & Buckner 2024, arXiv 2405.03207 (**Part II**, "The Way Forward"); the "new frontiers" half — benchmarks-vs-constructs, mechanistic interpretability (incl. the Othello-GPT world-model case study), LLM-as-agent-component, consciousness/self-report, the reproducibility crisis, and a "broadly negative (with qualifications)" verdict on LLMs as lookup tables / cognitive models. Completes the two-part survey backbone; refines the grounding / compositionality / deflationary concept pages; no empirical claims of its own. **status: received** (abstract + 8 section-level quotes verbatim from the ar5iv rendering of v1, 2026-06-13; no PDF page numbers — section locators only). (**philosophical track**)
- [`base/sources/beckmann-queloz-2025-mechanistic-indicators.md`](base/sources/beckmann-queloz-2025-mechanistic-indicators.md) — Beckmann & Queloz 2025, arXiv 2507.08017 (v5), "Mechanistic Indicators of Understanding in Large Language Models"; fuses **mechanistic interpretability** with a philosophical theory of understanding and proposes a **tiered framework** (conceptual → state-of-the-world → principled understanding, each tied to a level of computational organization). Argues the deflationary "merely imitating … without genuine understanding" picture is "increasingly untenable" and that we should **transcend binary "does AI understand?" debates** for a "comparative, mechanistically grounded epistemology" — a published anti-binary stance allied to the project's "describe, don't litigate," but read from the **mechanistic** side (the project's evidence is behavioral): a **map and interpretability-side counterpoint, not a human anchor**. Notes LLMs "diverge from human cognition in their parallel exploitation of heterogeneous mechanisms." **status: received** (abstract verbatim from the arXiv abs page 2026-06-14; §5/§6 bodies unreachable — both HTML renderings truncate inside §4, and the two disagree on the §5 title — so body catalogued at abstract-plus-structure level only). (**philosophical track**)
- [`base/sources/grindrod-2024-linguistic-intentionality.md`](base/sources/grindrod-2024-linguistic-intentionality.md) — Grindrod 2024, *Synthese* 204:71 (arXiv 2404.09576), "Large language models and linguistic intentionality"; argues the LLM meaningful-usage question is better posed at the **linguistic**-metasemantic level (how a *linguistic item* has content) than the **mental**-metasemantic one (how a *mental state* does), and that on Evans' naming-practices account and Millikan's teleosemantics LLM outputs come out **meaningful** — because linguistic intentionality is constitutively *dependent on a pre-existing linguistic system* the model inherits from its corpus. A hedged-positive, anti-deflation argument from the **philosophy-of-language** side (communicative intentions left open) — pairs with [`source/beckmann-queloz-2025-mechanistic-indicators`](base/sources/beckmann-queloz-2025-mechanistic-indicators.md) (anti-deflation from the *mechanistic* side) and triangulates with [`source/piantadosi-hill-2022-meaning-without-reference`](base/sources/piantadosi-hill-2022-meaning-without-reference.md) + [`source/schuele-2025-semantics-of-llms`](base/sources/schuele-2025-semantics-of-llms.md) on the "yes, but not by fixing reference" position. **Map/counterpoint, not a human anchor** (no annotated resource; reports no experiments); the project's own stance stays descriptivist. **status: received** (abstract + 6 §-located body quotes verified character-for-character against the accepted-version PDF, arxiv.org/pdf/2404.09576, 2026-06-14; one abs-page vs PDF model-name discrepancy flagged in-page). (**philosophical track**)
- [`base/sources/brennan-clark-1996-conceptual-pacts.md`](base/sources/brennan-clark-1996-conceptual-pacts.md) — Brennan & Clark 1996, *JEP:LMC* 22(6):1482–1493, "Conceptual Pacts and Lexical Choice in Conversation"; the **conceptual-pact** primary source (third-party course-site mirror PDF verified — the right paper, not Brennan 1996). Grounds the human side of the relational axis **on the partner dimension** (48% vs 18% term retention same- vs switched-partner; pacts established jointly), with the honest limit that it tests **historicity/partner-indexing, not order-sensitivity** ("Frequency of use better explains our data than does simple recency") — so the commutative-convention conjecture's "humans non-commutative" clause stays only partly grounded. **status: received** (page-level quotes verbatim from the PDF, 2026-06-12). (**relational axis**)
- [`base/sources/barrie-tornberg-2025-data-leakage.md`](base/sources/barrie-tornberg-2025-data-leakage.md) — Barrie & Törnberg 2025 (arXiv 2505.23796), "Emergent LLM behaviors are observationally equivalent to data leakage," **plus the authors' reply** (Flint Ashery, Aiello & Baronchelli 2025, arXiv 2506.18600). The **data-leakage critique of the in-repo [`source/ashery-2025-llm-conventions`](base/sources/ashery-2025-llm-conventions.md)** naming-game result (the relational axis's load-bearing LLM-side prior art) and its rebuttal — an **unadjudicated exchange** the project does not take a side in. Satisfies the `wanted.md` caveat that both sides be catalogued before any in-repo finding leans on the *emergence* (vs the mere occurrence) of LLM conventions; the project's own relational pilot/perturbation results make **no emergence claim**, so this calibrates rather than undermines them. **status: received** (2026-06-13, both abstracts verbatim + 6 section-level body quotes verified character-for-character against arXiv v1 HTML of each). (**relational axis / philosophical track**)
- [`base/sources/zeng-2026-lvlms-ground-differently.md`](base/sources/zeng-2026-lvlms-ground-differently.md) — Zeng et al. 2026, arXiv 2601.19792, "LVLMs and Humans Ground Differently in Referential Communication"; a referential-communication study collecting **human-human, human-AI, and AI-AI dyads in one paradigm** (356 dialogues; co-author Susan Brennan, of the conceptual-pacts source) — its advance over the model-only dyad papers ([`source/imai-2025-vlm-common-ground`](base/sources/imai-2025-vlm-common-ground.md), [`source/ashery-2025-llm-conventions`](base/sources/ashery-2025-llm-conventions.md)) is the same-paradigm human baseline. Finds even frontier GPT-5.2 "showed no hint of any ability to build common ground" and AI-director pairs "remarkably verbose," while humans rapidly entrain on compact reusable expressions — qualitatively **supports** the project's relational null's convergence-without-human-like-compression pattern ([`result/relational-reference-game-v1`](findings/results/relational-reference-game-v1.md)). Methodology is **both** discriminative (matcher selection) and generative (director production); has **no order-scramble control**, so it leaves the project's live-vs-shuffled wedge untouched. **Map/qualitative-support, not an `anchors:` resource** (experiment paper, not a standalone human-labeled asset). **status: received** (5 quotes verified character-for-character against abs page + HTML v3, 2026-06-15; per-condition counts and follow-up-model details flagged as section-level paraphrase). (**relational axis**)
- [`base/sources/mandelkern-linzen-2024-do-words-refer.md`](base/sources/mandelkern-linzen-2024-do-words-refer.md) — Mandelkern & Linzen 2024 (arXiv 2308.05576; *Computational Linguistics* 50(3) per publisher, unverified against arXiv metadata — flagged in-page), "Do Language Models' Words Refer?"; the strongest in-repo **pro-reference** argument: drawing on externalist metasemantics (Putnam/Kripke), it argues LMs' words *may* genuinely refer because training-text forms carry "natural histories of meaningful use" that tie them "eventually, to the referents" — relocating reference-fixing off the individual speaker. Runs the *same* externalist premise as [`concept/referential-meaning`](base/concepts/referential-meaning.md) to the *opposite* verdict (that page reads externalism as the strongest in-principle case an LLM does *not* refer), so the two are a productive tension a finding can cite from both poles; the referential-axis sibling of [`source/grindrod-2024-linguistic-intentionality`](base/sources/grindrod-2024-linguistic-intentionality.md) and the explicit denier of the no-reference premise [`source/piantadosi-hill-2022-meaning-without-reference`](base/sources/piantadosi-hill-2022-meaning-without-reference.md) *grants*. Verdict is explicitly **modal** ("may suffice," "looks much more likely") with a named speech-community escape hatch. **Map/interlocutor, not a human anchor** (conceptual argument; no experiments, no annotated resource). **status: received** (abstract + 9 section-located quotes verified verbatim against arXiv abs page + ar5iv HTML, 2026-06-15; CL venue + page numbers unverified — section locators only). (**philosophical track**)
- [`base/sources/baggio-murphy-2024-internalist-rejoinder.md`](base/sources/baggio-murphy-2024-internalist-rejoinder.md) — Baggio & Murphy 2024 (arXiv 2406.00159), "On the referential capacity of language models: An internalist rejoinder to Mandelkern & Linzen"; the published **internalist** rebuttal to [`source/mandelkern-linzen-2024-do-words-refer`](base/sources/mandelkern-linzen-2024-do-words-refer.md) (a direct `contradicts`). Runs the *opposite* metasemantics (Chomsky/Pietroski/Jackendoff internalism) to the *opposite* verdict on the same case: M&L's externalist argument is granted only for "a narrow class of natural language expressions" (§3), the "natural histories" of tokenised text are "neither natural, nor historical" since tokenisers cut across the units that bear histories (§4), and the bottom line is "Neither language models themselves can refer, and nor can 'their words' refer" (§4) — granting LMs only *aboutness*, not reference (§5). Pole-against-pole with M&L; sharpens [`concept/referential-meaning`](base/concepts/referential-meaning.md)'s internalism/externalism axis with a live published internalist voice, and fires revision-trigger (d) of [`essay/reference-as-premise-bound`](findings/essays/reference-as-premise-bound.md). **Map/interlocutor, not a human anchor** (conceptual argument; no experiments/annotations). **status: received** (8 §-located quotes verified character-for-character against the arXiv PDF via pdfminer, 2026-06-15; arXiv preprint, peer-review status unconfirmed — section locators only). (**philosophical track**)
- [`base/sources/ostertag-2025-externalist-reply.md`](base/sources/ostertag-2025-externalist-reply.md) — Ostertag 2025, *Computational Linguistics* 51(2):651–659 (ACL Anthology 2025.cl-2.8; DOI 10.1162/coli_a_00551), "Language Models and Externalism: A Reply to Mandelkern and Linzen"; the **third pole** in the in-repo LM-reference debate and a direct `contradicts` of [`source/mandelkern-linzen-2024-do-words-refer`](base/sources/mandelkern-linzen-2024-do-words-refer.md) — but an **intramural-externalist** one. Ostertag is *not* a defender of M&L and *not* an internalist: he grants externalism and the careful conditional, and argues only that M&L's particular "naïve externalist" route (bare natural history grounds reference) **fails on its own terms** — Lipton's contrastive-explanation test exposes a difference-maker the naïve account cannot supply ("oxygen is equally implicated in the causal history of water," §2), so "externalism, as understood by Mandelkern and Linzen, cannot ground reference" (§3). Explicitly accepts the conditional and doubts only the antecedent (§4: "my concern is not with the conditional, which I accept, but with the antecedent"), which independently exhibits the premise-bound shape [`essay/reference-as-premise-bound`](findings/essays/reference-as-premise-bound.md) diagnoses; fired/corrected that essay's trigger (e). **Does NOT cite or engage Baggio & Murphy** (no typed link between the two replies). **Map/interlocutor, not a human anchor** (conceptual argument; no experiments/annotations). **status: received** (10 page-located quotes verified character-for-character against the publisher PDF via pdfminer, 2026-06-15; peer-reviewed CL version of record). (**philosophical track**)
- [`base/sources/li-2024-cot-serial.md`](base/sources/li-2024-cot-serial.md) — Li, Liu, Zhou & Ma 2024, **ICLR 2024** (arXiv 2402.12875), "Chain of Thought Empowers Transformers to Solve Inherently Serial Problems"; a theoretical-CS expressiveness result: a constant-depth ("one forward pass") decoder-only transformer is confined to `AC^0`/`TC^0`, but with `T` chain-of-thought steps it can compute any size-`T` boolean circuit — so CoT supplies the **inherently serial computation** a single pass lacks, and helps most on hard-to-parallelize tasks, the first-named being **the composition of permutation groups**. The **formal counterpart** of the [`essay/output-channel-confound`](findings/essays/output-channel-confound.md) mechanism (a working surface lets a model perform serial computation a forced single token cannot) and the natural backdrop for the project's non-commuting-permutation composition probes (STEP/FLIP, CYCLE/SWAP on D4/A4/D6) — `supports` that essay, `refines` [`concept/formal-vs-functional-competence`](base/concepts/formal-vs-functional-competence.md). **Theory/mechanism source, not a human anchor and not a claim about the panel** (asymptotic, idealized-transformer; licenses no human comparison). **status: received** (abstract verbatim from the arXiv abs page 2026-06-19; body section-located via arXiv HTML / ar5iv, with a §3.4 locator correction logged in-page). (**methodology / philosophical track**)
- [`base/sources/he-2025-defeating-nondeterminism.md`](base/sources/he-2025-defeating-nondeterminism.md) — He & Thinking Machines Lab 2025, "Defeating Nondeterminism in LLM Inference" (open-access engineering blog, *Connectionism*, 2025-09-10); the **mechanism** source for temperature-0 nondeterminism. Diagnoses why greedy temp-0 decoding is not bit-reproducible in served inference: **not** per-kernel randomness (the forward-pass kernels are themselves run-to-run deterministic) but **load-dependent batch-size variation × non-batch-invariant kernels** — the same input reduces in a different order, hence a different rounded logit, depending on the batch it was served in; floating-point non-associativity (`(a+b)+c ≠ a+(b+c)`) is the ultimate numeric cause, and the often-blamed *concurrency* the lesser factor. `supports` [`findings/essays/point-estimate-is-a-draw.md`](findings/essays/point-estimate-is-a-draw.md) — **discharges its trigger (c)** (grounds *why* the temp-0 jitter occurs, not only *that* it does). **Mechanism source, not a human anchor and not a claim about the panel's batching** (an open-ended-generation setting; it grounds the *mechanism*, not the *magnitude* of label jitter on the project's forced-choice instruments — that stays the K=5 measurement). **status: received** (4 core quotes returned to a direct exact-wording WebFetch request 2026-06-21; not character-verified against raw HTML — flagged in-page). (**methodology / philosophical track**)
- [`base/sources/davis-2024-implicature-sep.md`](base/sources/davis-2024-implicature-sep.md) — Davis 2024, *Stanford Encyclopedia of Philosophy* (Fall 2025 archived edition; first pub. 2005, subst. rev. Jan 10 2024), "Implicature"; the **open-access semantics/pragmatics typology** of *what is said* vs *what is implicated* — conversational (incl. generalized/**scalar**) vs **conventional** implicature, with the standard diagnostics (cancelability; calculability; that "many believe … conversational implicatures cannot be" entailed by what is said, §2). Ingested to ground **essay trigger (d)** of [`essay/function-words-not-one-category`](findings/essays/function-words-not-one-category.md): an *a-priori* frame for why a truth-conditional/entailment instrument (3-way NLI) registers at-issue swaps (`some`→`every`) but legitimately diverges on a **scalar-implicature** one (`few`→`many`, [`result/function-word-few-many-split`](findings/results/function-word-few-many-split.md)). A typology about **human language, not LLMs** (applied as an interpretive frame only); itself contested in places ("exceptions have been noted"); `because`→`although` flagged as a *mixed* (not pure-implicature) case. **Map/interpretive frame, not a human anchor** (survey article; no annotated resource). **status: received** (11 §-located quotes verified verbatim against the archived edition URL, author confirmed via the citation-info page, 2026-06-21). (**philosophical track / constructional line**)
- [`base/sources/hitchcock-redei-2020-reichenbach-cc.md`](base/sources/hitchcock-redei-2020-reichenbach-cc.md) — Hitchcock & Rédei 2020, *Stanford Encyclopedia of Philosophy* (first pub. Jan 13, 2020), "Reichenbach's Common Cause Principle"; the **open-access methodology source** on **common-cause-vs-coincidence inference** — when two correlated events neither of which causes the other license positing a **common cause** that **screens them off** (renders them *conditionally independent*), and the §5 counterexamples that bound the inference. Ingested to **partially discharge revision trigger (e)** of [`essay/cross-level-convergence-ladder`](findings/essays/cross-level-convergence-ladder.md): it **confirms** that the ladder's R1→R2 (instrument-equalization) step is the behavioral form of Reichenbach's **screening-off / independence** requirement, and **relocates** the bar (the principle is *more permissive* — a robust correlation already licenses a common-cause hypothesis — so the ladder is read as a deliberately conservative behavioral specialization, not a refuted yardstick). **Methodology source, not a human anchor** (encyclopedia entry; no annotated resource; licenses no LLM claim). **status: received** (5 short passages verbatim, double-fetch-confirmed + independently spot-checked against the SEP page, 2026-06-22; entry not read in full — deeper §3/§4 formal material not catalogued). (**methodology / philosophical track**)
- [`base/sources/heesen-bright-zucker-2019-triangulation.md`](base/sources/heesen-bright-zucker-2019-triangulation.md) — Heesen, Bright & Zucker 2019, *Synthese* 196(8):3067–3081 (CC BY 4.0); the **open-access methodology source** on **methodological triangulation / variety-of-evidence** — using multiple methods at once so that, under uncertainty about any one method's reliability, agreement "is confirmed more strongly than it could have been by any single method"; a voting-theory result shows Du Boisian triangulation beats "purism" "assuming the scientist is subject to some degree of diffidence", and "even when in fact only one of the methods is appropriate". Ingested to **more fully discharge revision trigger (e)** of [`essay/cross-level-convergence-ladder`](findings/essays/cross-level-convergence-ladder.md): it grounds the ladder's R1→R2 step from the **variety-of-evidence** angle (agreement across genuinely-different methods is confirmatory) — a second external confirmation alongside Reichenbach's screening-off — while again **relocating** the bar more permissively (triangulation is vindicated under mere diffidence), so the ladder stays a deliberately conservative behavioral specialization. **Methodology source, not a human anchor** (no annotated resource; licenses no LLM claim). **status: received** (abstract-level provenance — the OA abstract is text-readable and double-fetch-confirmed; full-text PDFs are image-based / un-quotable, 2026-06-22). (**methodology / philosophical track**)
- [`base/sources/sennet-2021-ambiguity-sep.md`](base/sources/sennet-2021-ambiguity-sep.md) — Sennet 2021, *Stanford Encyclopedia of Philosophy* (Summer 2021 Edition; first pub. May 16 2011, subst. rev. May 22 2021), "Ambiguity"; the **open-access philosophy-of-language reference** for the **homonymy/polysemy carving** ("ambiguity in words is a matter of two or more lexical entries that correspond to the same word and polysemy a single lexeme that has multiple meanings"; polysemy = senses "in some hard to specify sense, interestingly related"), the **ambiguity-vs-vagueness/generality** distinction ('bat' ambiguous, 'is bald' vague), and the **zeugma / conjunction-reduction diagnostic** (reliable "in clear cases," fragile "in controversial cases"). Ingested to **discharge the in-repo-source gap** the concept page's *Honest gaps* and the essay's provenance note both name: it grounds the **scalar (polysemy, related senses, nearer pole) vs. disjunctive (homonymy, distinct entries, no nearer pole)** carving that [`essay/ambiguity-kind-not-level`](findings/essays/ambiguity-kind-not-level.md) leans on — `supports` [`concept/polysemy`](base/concepts/polysemy.md) and that essay. Carries Sennet's own caveat that the carving is "one traditional carving," not a sharp formal partition (consistent with the project's gradience framing). **Does NOT** replace the still-wanted Cruse/Murphy/Lyons monographs, and **does NOT** discharge the *regular/systematic (Apresjan) polysemy* want (the entry, as fetched, does not develop that terminology — left open). **Map/reference, not a human anchor** (philosophy survey; no LLM claim, no annotated resource — cannot serve as an `anchors:` resource). **status: received** (7 key quotes double-fetch-confirmed verbatim across the live + Summer-2021-archived URLs, 2026-06-22; one §4.7 tail trimmed for double-fetch disagreement and the zeugma example sentences left out as single-fetch-only — both flagged in-page). (**philosophical track / lexical line**)
- [`base/sources/falkum-vicente-2015-polysemy.md`](base/sources/falkum-vicente-2015-polysemy.md) — Falkum & Vicente 2015, *Lingua* 157:1–16 (editorial to the special issue on polysemy; DOI 10.1016/j.lingua.2015.02.002; green-OA author-postprint via PhilArchive `FALPCP.pdf`). The **regular/systematic (Apresjan) polysemy** ingest that [`source/sennet-2021-ambiguity-sep`](base/sources/sennet-2021-ambiguity-sep.md) and the [`essay/ambiguity-kind-not-level`](findings/essays/ambiguity-kind-not-level.md) honesty box both flagged as still-open: it states the **regular/logical vs. irregular/accidental** carving ("customary … to distinguish between regular or logical polysemy … and irregular or accidental polysemy"; the Apresjan-1974 criterion), gives **logical polysemy** as the sub-class "operationally defined as polysemy which passes the conjunction and anaphoric reference tests," ties regular polysemy to **rule-generated productivity** + metonymy, and carries the honesty caveat that "the distinction between regular and irregular polysemy is not clear-cut either." A *patterned* species of the **scalar/related** pole, not a new disjunctive kind. **Map/reference, not a human anchor** (a survey editorial about human language; no annotated resource — cannot serve as an `anchors:` resource). Discharges the **conceptual carving + productive-pattern** part of the regular-polysemy want; does **not** discharge the still-wanted Cruse/Murphy/Lyons monographs or supply a graded instrument. `supports` [`concept/polysemy`](base/concepts/polysemy.md) + [`essay/ambiguity-kind-not-level`](findings/essays/ambiguity-kind-not-level.md). **status: received** (3 load-bearing quotes double-confirmed verbatim across mirrors; 2 column-scrambled passages flagged as paraphrase not quoted, 2026-06-23). (**philosophical track / lexical line**)
- [`base/sources/pustejovsky-1991-generative-lexicon.md`](base/sources/pustejovsky-1991-generative-lexicon.md) — Pustejovsky 1991, *Computational Linguistics* 17(4):409–441 (ACL Anthology J91-4003; open access). The founding **Generative Lexicon** paper — the locus classicus for the **contrastive (accidental / homonymy) vs. complementary (logical-polysemy) ambiguity** distinction (citing Weinreich 1972: *bank* river/institution = accidental homonymy; institution/building = logical polysemy), **qualia structure**, and **type coercion / logical metonymy** ("Mary enjoyed the book"). Supplies the *rival-vs-co-active* theoretical backbone for the **forced-both** wedge: a balanced homonym is *contrastive* (one reading operative on resolution), a forced-both pun/zeugma is *complementary* (senses jointly required) — the distinction [`essay/layer-specialness-vs-always-resolvability`](findings/essays/layer-specialness-vs-always-resolvability.md) flagged as its weakest provenance point, and the principled basis for the [`decisions/resolved/forced-both-lexical-operationalization`](decisions/resolved/forced-both-lexical-operationalization.md) Q1 zeugma/co-predication diagnostics. **Honesty note:** the *term* "copredication" and the **dot-object/dot-type** apparatus are Pustejovsky's *later* (GL 1995) work, NOT this 1991 article — the page quotes only the 1991 text and flags the 1995 attributions. Complements [`source/falkum-vicente-2015-polysemy`](base/sources/falkum-vicente-2015-polysemy.md) (the survey-side regular/logical carving + the conjunction/anaphora copredication diagnostics this machinery underwrites). **Map/reference, not a human anchor** (formal-semantics theory; no LLM claim, no annotated resource). `supports` [`concept/polysemy`](base/concepts/polysemy.md) + the essay. **status: received** (10 verbatim passages with printed-page locators extracted from the ACL Anthology PDF text layer via pdfminer, whitespace-normalized as declared, 2026-06-23). (**philosophical track / lexical line**)
- [`base/sources/cronbach-meehl-1955-construct-validity.md`](base/sources/cronbach-meehl-1955-construct-validity.md) — Cronbach & Meehl 1955, *Psychological Bulletin* 52(4):281–302 (open-access York mirror, "Classics in the History of Psychology"; © 1955 APA, not public-domain). The **founding methodology statement of construct validity**: the four validation types (predictive/concurrent = **criterion-oriented**; content; **construct**), the rule that "Construct validity must be investigated whenever no criterion or universe of content is accepted as entirely adequate to define the quality to be measured," the **nomological-network** account (a construct is validated by its place in "the interlocking system of laws which constitute a theory"; "'Learning more about' a … construct is a matter of elaborating the nomological network"), and the **three-way charge of negative evidence** (a disconfirmation may be charged to the test, the theory/net, or the design — "any link in the chain may be wrong"). Ingested to ground [`essay/construct-validity-without-a-criterion`](findings/essays/construct-validity-without-a-criterion.md) and to discharge the "weakest provenance point" both [`essay/no-admissible-certifier`](findings/essays/no-admissible-certifier.md) and [`essay/design-out-not-model-out`](findings/essays/design-out-not-model-out.md) flagged. **Methodology anchor, NOT a human-comparison anchor** (a 1955 measurement paper; no LLM claim, no annotated resource — cannot serve as an `anchors:` resource). Does **not** introduce convergent/discriminant validity (Campbell & Fiske 1959, now in-repo — see below) or construct-irrelevant-variance/under-representation (Messick 1995, now in-repo — see below) — both are later refinements. **status: received** (verbatim quotes character-verified locally against the mirror HTML; section-heading locators, mirror unpaginated, 2026-06-23). (**methodology / philosophical track**)
- [`base/sources/ortega-andres-2020-copredication.md`](base/sources/ortega-andres-2020-copredication.md) — Ortega Andrés 2020, "Polysemous Nouns and Copredication" (PhD thesis, UPV/EHU; supervisor A. Vicente; open institutional-repository, ADDI). The **copredication-by-name** ingest that the [`source/pustejovsky-1991-generative-lexicon`](base/sources/pustejovsky-1991-generative-lexicon.md) honesty note and the [`essay/layer-specialness-vs-always-resolvability`](findings/essays/layer-specialness-vs-always-resolvability.md) provenance note both flagged as still-open: it **defines copredication** ("the same polysemous nominal expression comes along with simultaneous predications for two (or more) different … senses … in a sentence"), states **copredication as a diagnostic** for sense *availability*, and frames the **polysemy↔homonymy distinction as a continuum** — closely-related polysemous senses "activate each other, forming activation packages that facilitate copredication," while "meanings of homonymous words inhibit each other" — i.e. the **forced-both (co-active) vs. rival (inhibitory/pickable)** poles the forced-both wedge rests on, with the honesty caveat that copredicability "is … a question of degree rather than an all-or-nothing matter." The **zeugma** term stays grounded by [`source/sennet-2021-ambiguity-sep`](base/sources/sennet-2021-ambiguity-sep.md) (the thesis does not use it). The published *Glossa* article (Ortega-Andrés & Vicente 2019, CC-BY) remains **un-ingested / still-wanted** (glossa-journal.org Anubis-gated to automated fetch). **Map/reference, not a human anchor** (a thesis about human language; no LLM claim, no annotated resource). `supports` [`concept/polysemy`](base/concepts/polysemy.md) + the two essays above. **status: received** (verbatim quotes extracted locally from the openly-downloaded PDF with declared ligature/line-break normalization, 2026-06-23). (**philosophical track / lexical line**)
- [`base/sources/messick-1995-validity-of-psychological-assessment.md`](base/sources/messick-1995-validity-of-psychological-assessment.md) — Messick 1995, *American Psychologist* 50(9):741–749. The canonical statement of **unified validity** — validity as a single integrated **construct-validity** concept of which content, criteria, and consequences are aspects, not separate substitutable types; validity is "not a property of the test … but rather of the meaning of the test scores." The source that **defines the project's two key threat terms** — **construct underrepresentation** ("the assessment is too narrow and fails to include important dimensions … of the construct") and **construct-irrelevant variance** ("the assessment is too broad, containing excess reliable variance … irrelevant to the interpreted construct"). Ingested to let [`essay/construct-validity-without-a-criterion`](findings/essays/construct-validity-without-a-criterion.md) state its *design-out-not-model-out* → construct-irrelevant-variance and *presence-is-not-balance* → construct-underrepresentation mappings in Messick's precise post-1955 vocabulary (the essay's trigger (d)). **Methodology anchor, NOT a human-comparison anchor**; © 1995 APA, open-access Bath mirror, 17 verbatim quotes grep-verified locally. `depends-on`/companion to [`source/cronbach-meehl-1955-construct-validity`](base/sources/cronbach-meehl-1955-construct-validity.md). **status: received** (2026-06-24). (**philosophical track / methodology line**)
- [`base/sources/freiesleben-2026-construct-validity-llm-benchmarks.md`](base/sources/freiesleben-2026-construct-validity-llm-benchmarks.md) — Freiesleben 2026, arXiv:2603.15121v1 [cs.LG]. A philosophy-of-measurement position paper arguing that for **capabilities attributed to LLMs from benchmark scores**, Cronbach & Meehl's **nomological-network account** "provides the most suitable foundation," over **Borsboom's causal/realist account** (too ontologically demanding for LLMs) and the **Messick/Kane inferential account** ("offers limited resources for even theorizing the construct"). The LLM-domain companion to the Cronbach-Meehl ingest: an **independent peer reaching the project's own framing choice** (nomological-net construct validity is the right frame when no single criterion is available), plus a citable **secondary** engagement with Messick's and Borsboom's accounts (both flagged as Freiesleben's characterization, never as primaries). §3.1 "design nomological networks prior to benchmarks" rhymes with the project's *freeze-before-run* gate; §3.4 frames theory–measurement conflict as Duhem–Quine, echoing the three-way negative-evidence charge. **arXiv preprint (peer-review unconfirmed); methodology + peer-positioning source, NOT a human anchor.** 16 verbatim quotes grep-verified locally. `supports` [`essay/construct-validity-without-a-criterion`](findings/essays/construct-validity-without-a-criterion.md). **status: received** (2026-06-24). (**philosophical track / methodology line**)
- [`base/sources/borsboom-2004-concept-of-validity.md`](base/sources/borsboom-2004-concept-of-validity.md) — Borsboom, Mellenbergh & van Heerden 2004, *Psychological Review* 111(4):1061–1071 (open-access author mirror dennyborsboom.com; © 2004 APA; sha256-pinned). The **realist/causal critique** of the construct-validity tradition — "a test is valid for measuring an attribute if and only if (a) the attribute exists and (b) variations in the attribute causally produce variations in the outcomes of the measurement procedure" (p.1061); "Validity is not a judgment at all. It is the property being judged" (p.1063, vs Messick); the nomological network dismissed as a logical-positivist "relic" (p.1063), with the decisive objection "Few, if any, theoretical terms in psychology can be unambiguously identified in this way" (p.1064). The **primary** for [`essay/construct-validity-without-a-criterion`](findings/essays/construct-validity-without-a-criterion.md)'s **trigger (e)** "second amputation" leg (the causal/realist validation route the project's deflationary commitment bars), previously in-repo only via Freiesleben's secondary rendering — **confirmed faithful** (the iff-thesis + the "Few, if any…" line match), so the essay's argument needs only a secondary→primary citation upgrade, no correction. `contradicts` [`source/cronbach-meehl-1955-construct-validity`](base/sources/cronbach-meehl-1955-construct-validity.md) + [`source/messick-1995-validity-of-psychological-assessment`](base/sources/messick-1995-validity-of-psychological-assessment.md); `refines` [`source/freiesleben-2026-construct-validity-llm-benchmarks`](base/sources/freiesleben-2026-construct-validity-llm-benchmarks.md). Also supplies Borsboom's primary one-liner on MTMM ("a favorable matrix configuration is not constitutive of validity", p.1068); **Campbell & Fiske 1959** itself is now in-repo (see below). **Methodology anchor, NOT a human-comparison anchor** (no LLM claim; licenses no realist commitment about models). **status: received** (13 verbatim quotes grep-verified locally against the author-mirror PDF, journal-page locators, 2026-06-24, session 97). (**philosophical track / methodology line**)
- [`base/sources/campbell-fiske-1959-mtmm.md`](base/sources/campbell-fiske-1959-mtmm.md) — Campbell & Fiske 1959, *Psychological Bulletin* 56(2):81–105 (open-access UBC psychology course mirror; © 1959 APA, not public-domain; sha256-pinned). The **primary statement of the multitrait–multimethod (MTMM) matrix** and the paired **convergent / discriminant validation** vocabulary: convergent validation is "a confirmation by independent measurement procedures" (p.81) and discriminant validation is "required" alongside it (p.81); each measure is a "**trait-method unit**, a union of a particular trait content with measurement procedures not specific to that content" (p.81), so "irrelevant method variance … these scores are invalid" (p.84); reliability vs. validity placed on one method-similarity continuum (p.83); and the asymmetry that "convergence between two is a satisfactory minimal requirement" while "Discriminative validation is not so easily achieved" and "one can never establish that a trait, as measured, is differentiated from all other traits" (p.103). Ingested to discharge the **Campbell & Fiske leg of [`essay/construct-validity-without-a-criterion`](findings/essays/construct-validity-without-a-criterion.md) trigger (e)** (session 98) — the MTMM vocabulary now enters at **primary** strength, not via Messick's citation or Borsboom's one-line critic's verdict (the secondary characterizations confirmed consistent, no correction); the trait-method-unit insight backs the project's *design-out-not-model-out* worry and the cross-method-convergence preference maps to the [`convergence ladder`](findings/essays/cross-level-convergence-ladder.md)'s R1→R2 rungs. Companion-primary to [`source/cronbach-meehl-1955-construct-validity`](base/sources/cronbach-meehl-1955-construct-validity.md) (Campbell & Fiske build on and quote it, p.83). **Methodology anchor, NOT a human-comparison anchor** (a 1959 measurement paper; no LLM claim, no annotated resource — cannot serve as an `anchors:` resource; the MTMM matrix is a tool for *evidence*, not a *constitution* of validity, per Borsboom's standing objection). **status: received** (18 verbatim quotes grep-verified locally against the mirror PDF, journal-page locators, 2026-06-24, session 98). (**philosophical track / methodology line**)

### Base — resources

- [`base/resources/index.md`](base/resources/index.md) — catalog of human-anchored empirical resources.
- [`base/resources/subtlex-us-frequency.md`](base/resources/subtlex-us-frequency.md) — **SUBTLEX-US word-frequency norm** (Brysbaert & New 2009; 74,286 word forms from a 51M-word subtitle corpus; `Lg10WF` = log10 word-form frequency). Status: **catalogued** (plain-text list fetched + sha256-pinned this session; no formal license string — recipe-not-corpus: full list gitignored, `prep.py` + a derived seed table committed). The **Q1 frequency-matching floor** for [`conjecture/function-word-substitutability`](findings/conjectures/function-word-substitutability.md), governed by [`decisions/resolved/function-word-anchor-design`](decisions/resolved/function-word-anchor-design.md) (**ratified 2026-06-21**). Grounds the matching *control*, not the indicator (no PoS/acceptability/entailment). (created 2026-06-21)
- [`base/resources/languageR-dative-corpus.md`](base/resources/languageR-dative-corpus.md) — **Bresnan et al. (2007) dative-alternation corpus** (`languageR::dative`; GPL; 3263 attested ditransitive clauses coded for the information-structure factors — given/accessible/new, pronominality, definiteness, animacy, length — plus the NP/PP outcome). Documentation + license verified verbatim from CRAN; **mirrored + inspected firsthand 2026-06-20 (status catalogued)** — 3263×15 confirmed, NP(DOC)=2414/PP(PD)=849, factor levels confirmed, logistic fit reproduces the canonical human directions (acc 0.887). Anchors [`conjecture/dative-alternation-information-structure`](findings/conjectures/dative-alternation-information-structure.md); the build is governed by [`decisions/resolved/dative-anchor-and-indicator`](decisions/resolved/dative-anchor-and-indicator.md) (**ratified 2026-06-20, ADOPT MODIFIED** — corpus production surface adopted as primary anchor). (created 2026-06-20)
- [`base/resources/mahowald-2023-aann-stimuli.md`](base/resources/mahowald-2023-aann-stimuli.md) — Mahowald 2023 EACL AANN stimulus suite + MTurk acceptability ratings (status: **catalogued** 2026-06-12 — repo mirrored, MIT license verified, Exp-2 item-level ratings confirmed usable); anchor for [`conjecture/aann-construction`](findings/conjectures/aann-construction.md).
- [`base/resources/wic-graded-usage-similarity.md`](base/resources/wic-graded-usage-similarity.md) — Usim graded usage-similarity ratings (Erk, McCarthy & Gaylord 2009/2013) — graded 5-point human usage-similarity judgments; the candidate gradience anchor for [`conjecture/lexical-sense-gradience`](findings/conjectures/lexical-sense-gradience.md), with WiC (Pilehvar & Camacho-Collados 2019, binary, CC BY-NC 4.0) as the binary cross-check. Status: external-only (license/counts unverified this run — see page). (created 2026-05-29)
- [`base/resources/wic-word-in-context.md`](base/resources/wic-word-in-context.md) — **WiC (Word-in-Context, Pilehvar & Camacho-Collados 2019, NAACL; CC BY-NC 4.0).** **Verified live 2026-05-31** (package fetched + inspected; sha256 pinned): **binary** lexicographer same/different-sense labels over two contexts of a target word, 7,466 items (50/50, N+V, 2,345 targets; the pilehvar package **ships test gold labels**). Negatives are **homonymy-enriched** (closest-polyseme pairs pruned) — the discreteness contrast DWUG EN lacked. Scope limit: **binary, not graded** (no DURel-median correlation). Anchors the clause-(b) lexical-v3 ([`design/lexical-polysemy-homonymy-v3`](../experiments/designs/lexical-polysemy-homonymy-v3.md)) **and** the image probe ([`design/multimodal-grounding-image-v1`](../experiments/designs/multimodal-grounding-image-v1.md)). (created 2026-05-31)
- [`base/resources/semeval2017-pun-corpus.md`](base/resources/semeval2017-pun-corpus.md) — **SemEval-2017 Task 7 pun corpus** (Miller, Hempelmann & Gurevych 2017; mixed CC BY 4.0 / CC BY-NC 4.0; fetched + sha256-hashed + inspected firsthand 2026-06-23). ~1298 homographic + ~1098 heterographic puns with **human per-item gold of the two WordNet 3.1 senses each pun evokes, on the actual sentence** — human sense **co-activation** labels for genuine forced-both items (the in-item evidence SemCor's general-usage proxy could not give). Anchor for the forced-both line (gate Q4) + the matched-ambiguity Option-A homonym sense-anchor; **anchor RATIFIED for Q4 co-activation only, session 93** ([`decisions/resolved/sense-coactivation-anchor-semeval-puns`](decisions/resolved/sense-coactivation-anchor-semeval-puns.md); Q-A adopt / Q-B-1 separate dominance step owed / Q-C-1 puns as forced-both stimuli, homonym subset, frozen). Honest limit: certifies co-*presence*, not graded balance/dominance. (catalogued 2026-06-23, session 92)
- [`base/resources/homonym-meaning-dominance-norms.md`](base/resources/homonym-meaning-dominance-norms.md) — **Homonym meaning-dominance norms** (British eDom, Maciejewski & Klepousniotou 2016, 10.5334/jopd.28; + spoken-ambiguity norms, J. Cognition 10.5334/joc.194; both **CC BY 4.0**, licenses + OSF reachability + schema verified by direct fetch 2026-06-23). Per-**word** human sense-balance/dominance (D≈0 = balanced) for *selecting* balanced homonyms — the human-anchored balance/dominance step the [`decisions/resolved/sense-coactivation-anchor-semeval-puns`](decisions/resolved/sense-coactivation-anchor-semeval-puns.md) Q-B-1 calls for (ratified session 93 — a separate dominance step is owed since co-activation ≠ no-dominance); a CC-BY upgrade over the SemCor general-balance proxy. **General-usage, not the specific sentence's** balance → softens-not-eliminates the forced-both Q1-ii in-item gap; data not yet fetched. (catalogued 2026-06-23, session 92)
- [`base/resources/wordnet-sense-inventory.md`](base/resources/wordnet-sense-inventory.md) — **Princeton WordNet** (Miller 1995 / Fellbaum 1998; permissive WordNet 3.0 License, verified verbatim from the NLTK-shipped LICENSE). The expert-lexicographer **synset** sense inventory (117,659 synsets / 82,115 noun; verified via NLTK). The categorical same/different-sense backbone the op-gate Q2 + v2/v3 stratification assume; anchors the image probe's constructed pairs (gold = same vs different synset). Honest grain: categorical lexicographic partition, **not** graded (DWUG) nor per-item human labels (WiC). (created 2026-05-31)
- [`base/resources/dwug-usage-graphs.md`](base/resources/dwug-usage-graphs.md) — DWUG (Diachronic Word Usage Graphs, Schlechtweg et al.): graded human usage-similarity judgments in the DURel/Usim tradition; evaluated this session as the ratified **Option-B** graded-anchor candidate for [`conjecture/lexical-sense-gradience`](findings/conjectures/lexical-sense-gradience.md) — see the page for the license / scale / counts / fetchability / fit verification breakdown. (created 2026-05-30)
- [`base/resources/lancaster-sensorimotor-norms.md`](base/resources/lancaster-sensorimotor-norms.md) — Lancaster Sensorimotor Norms (Lynott et al. 2020, **CC BY 4.0**): human perceptual/action strength ratings (0–5) on 11 sensorimotor dimensions for 39,707 English words; **fetched + checksummed this session** (sha256 pinned; full CSV gitignored, derived 42-lemma join table committed). The text-side perceptual-grounding **moderator** for prediction 1 of [`conjecture/multimodal-lexical-grounding-divergence`](findings/conjectures/multimodal-lexical-grounding-divergence.md) — a $0 join to the existing DWUG lexical result. Word-level (not sense-level); bears on prediction 1 only, not the image predictions. (created 2026-05-30; **multimodal axis**)
- [`base/resources/multimodal-anchor-scouting.md`](base/resources/multimodal-anchor-scouting.md) — **scouting note** (untyped, `wanted.md`-style; not yet a typed resource) on candidate human-anchored multimodal/grounded resources. Verified license/fetchability/meaning-bearing for 6 candidates; headline: **Lancaster Sensorimotor Norms** (CC BY 4.0) as a $0 text-side perceptual-grounding moderator on the existing DWUG lexical result, and **THINGS-data** (CC0) for an image-grounded probe; Winoground/SNLI-VE dropped (gated/auto-derived). (created 2026-05-30; **multimodal axis**)
- [`base/resources/vwsd-semeval-2023.md`](base/resources/vwsd-semeval-2023.md) — **VWSD (SemEval-2023 Task 1, Raganato et al. 2023)** — the **image-native** word-sense-disambiguation anchor [`conjecture/distributional-saturation-grounding-headroom`](findings/conjectures/distributional-saturation-grounding-headroom.md) named (but no session had scouted) for its text-under-determined stratum: pick 1 of 10 images for an ambiguous word given minimal context (EN/IT/FA). **Human gold = test (463 EN / 200 FA / 305 IT) + trial (16 EN)** (annotators authored the trigger words + curated the 9 distractors); **training (12,869 EN) is silver/automatic — not an anchor**. License **CC-BY-NC 4.0** (task-website only; scope unspecified; **image-redistribution UNCONFIRMED** — third-party image sources Wikidata/OmegaWiki/BabelPic). **Fetchable now** via Drive/OneDrive (572 MB resized test), no registration; **not fetched/checksummed this session**. Honest limit: gold is **binary correct-image selection, not a graded relatedness signal** — supplies selection-accuracy, *not* a drop-in for the conjecture's DURel-style graded DV. **The DV gate is now resolved** ([`decisions/resolved/vwsd-grounding-headroom-dv`](decisions/resolved/vwsd-grounding-headroom-dv.md), ratified s99 ADOPT MODIFIED: Option A, the selection-accuracy × text-separability *interaction* as test of record, tests the gating *shape* NOT prediction-1-as-written). **status: scouted + catalogued** (2026-06-24, session 97; **multimodal axis**)
- [`base/resources/things-data-triplets.md`](base/resources/things-data-triplets.md) — **THINGS-data behavioral triplet odd-one-out judgments (Hebart et al. 2023, eLife 12:e82580)** — scouted s99 as a candidate **graded** multimodal anchor (the "future graded-image resource" the VWSD DV ratification reserved for prediction-1-as-written). 4.70M human odd-one-out similarity judgments (4,699,160) over 1,854 object concepts / 26,107 images, N=12,340. **Fit verdict: DOES NOT CLEANLY FIT (partial/adjacent)** — it supplies graded human *whole-object similarity* (which of three objects is most dissimilar), a **different construct** from the conjecture's graded *within-word sense relatedness with disambiguating images*; no same-word/different-sense pairs, no polysemy structure → **not** a drop-in for [`resource/dwug-usage-graphs`](base/resources/dwug-usage-graphs.md)'s graded sense anchor. Right *shape* (graded + image + human + multi-rater), wrong *axis* (object similarity ≠ sense relatedness). Could legitimately anchor a distinct **representational-alignment** question or serve as PD/CC0 stimulus scaffolding (via THINGSplus). License honesty: behavioral data **reported CC0 but NOT primary-verified** (OSF node_license=null; Figshare+ 403'd); base THINGS **images are academic-use-only/restricted** (THINGSplus supplies PD/CC0 images) — do not conflate. Not fetched/checksummed. **status: scouted** (2026-06-24, session 99; **multimodal axis**)
- [`base/resources/scivetti-2025-cxnli-dataset.md`](base/resources/scivetti-2025-cxnli-dataset.md) — Scivetti et al. 2025 CxNLI / CxNLI-Distinction constructional NLI dataset (435 + 99 triples over 8 / 5 constructions; native-speaker baseline ≈0.90 / ≈0.83). Status: partial (de-anonymized repo inspected 2026-05-29: per-item construction labels + single gold answer per item). **Ratified anchor (2026-05-29)** for the caused-motion, conative, way, and comparative-correlative conjectures — answer-key + aggregate baseline. (created 2026-05-29)
- [`base/resources/hawkins-tangrams.md`](base/resources/hawkins-tangrams.md) — **Hawkins/Stanford tangrams repeated-reference corpus** (Hawkins, Frank & Goodman 2020, *Cognitive Science*; GitHub `license: null` + authors' "open corpus" statement). **Fetched + verified 2026-05-31** (sha256 `db8cee9d…`, 3.13 MB, 17,431 messages / 137 dyads / repetitions 1–6; raw gitignored, derived aggregate entrainment table committed under the **recipe-not-corpus** posture). Carries **ordered per-dyad referring-expression histories** with role/success/length — the human entrainment/compression curve (length 7.73→4.10 words, accuracy 0.78→0.94 over 6 reps) the relational pilot's convergence baseline needs. **Anchors the human convergence baseline only** — the pilot's novel live-vs-shuffled *trajectory-dependence* measure is **not** anchored by Hawkins. Catalogued per [`decisions/resolved/relational-fetchable-anchor`](decisions/resolved/relational-fetchable-anchor.md) (Option A). (created 2026-05-31)
- [`base/resources/blimp.md`](base/resources/blimp.md) — **BLiMP (Benchmark of Linguistic Minimal Pairs, Warstadt et al. 2020, TACL 8; CC-BY, README-prose only).** 67 paradigms × 1,000 = **67,000** template-generated English acceptability minimal pairs over 12 phenomena (incl. determiner-noun agreement, quantifiers, NPI licensing, subject-verb agreement); **96.4% aggregate human agreement** (distinct from the 89% baseline the Mahowald source quotes — kept separate). Status: **catalogued** (67 data files fetched + field schema inspected firsthand; a 10-line sample sha256-pinned, full set re-fetchable not committed). CAN supply a human-**acceptability** forced-choice backing — the optional **Posture-2 upgrade** named in [`decisions/resolved/function-word-anchor-design`](decisions/resolved/function-word-anchor-design.md) (overlaps the swap targets via determiner-noun agreement / quantifiers / NPI), and an adjacent baseline for the AANN line; **CANNOT** anchor entailment/implicature/sense-similarity (acceptability ≠ inference) and is template-generated (contamination caveat). (created 2026-06-21)
- [`base/resources/scalar-implicature-anchor-scouting.md`](base/resources/scalar-implicature-anchor-scouting.md) — **scouting page** (front-mattered) for a human-grounded **scalar-implicature / quantifier-interpretation** anchor for [`essay/function-words-not-one-category`](findings/essays/function-words-not-one-category.md) trigger (b) (the few→many "Many X → All X" split, [`result/function-word-few-many-split`](findings/results/function-word-few-many-split.md)). Scouted van Tiel et al. 2016 scalar-diversity (on-target quantifier `<some,all>` rate, but paywalled / OA PDF 403), Pankratz & van Tiel 2025 (CC BY but adjectival, off-target), VAQUUM quantifier appropriateness (close but appropriateness ≠ implicature-rate, rating license unverified), and the in-repo Scivetti CxNLI (single gold label, no quantifiers). **Honest null:** no clean openly-licensed quantifier-specific human implicature-rate set found → trigger (b)'s human-comparison upgrade stays blocked; `internal-contrast-only` remains the honest posture. (created 2026-06-21)
