### Findings — conjectures

- [`findings/conjectures/cross-level-gradience-aggregate-not-moment.md`](findings/conjectures/cross-level-gradience-aggregate-not-moment.md) — status: **tested → DISSOLUTION** (2026-06-22, session 84); **RAN under the resolved gate → the shape does NOT survive instrument-equalization (3/3 models dissolve; discrete-on-moment only at the lexical level)** → [`result/cross-level-shared-instrument-v1`](findings/results/cross-level-shared-instrument-v1.md); the deflationary default stands. Originally the forward bet that the "**graded-in-the-aggregate, discrete-in-the-moment**" shape is **one cross-level property of distributional competence**, not three rhyming facts. Matures [`open-question/gradience-population-not-moment`](findings/open-questions/gradience-population-not-moment.md) into a **falsifiable, symmetric** bet: *confirm* = the two-axis dissociation **survives instrument-equalization** across ≥2 levels under one frozen shared instrument; *falsify (dissolution)* = it shows under each level's native instrument but **dissolves** when the instrument is equalized → three rhyming facts; anti-cheat against **per-level instrument-shopping**. `anchor: pending` — lexical leg capped to usage-similarity, constructional + relational `internal-contrast-only` → any unified claim only at the **weakest common strength**. Its operationalization gate [`decisions/resolved/cross-level-shared-instrument-operationalization`](decisions/resolved/cross-level-shared-instrument-operationalization.md) was **ratified session 82 (ADOPT DEFAULT)** → `contingent-on` cleared, status `designed`. `refines`/`depends-on` the OQ; `depends-on` [`result/lexical-bridging-context-v1`](findings/results/lexical-bridging-context-v1.md), [`result/lexical-bridging-context-working-surface-v1`](findings/results/lexical-bridging-context-working-surface-v1.md), [`concept/distributional-meaning`](base/concepts/distributional-meaning.md). A **non-spend** scoping unit. (created 2026-06-22; **cross-level synthesis**)
- [`findings/conjectures/dative-alternation-information-structure.md`](findings/conjectures/dative-alternation-information-structure.md)
- [`findings/conjectures/aann-construction.md`](findings/conjectures/aann-construction.md) — status: **tested — SUPPORTED** (2026-06-12: after the logprob v1 was retired unrun, the behavioral instrument was ratified ([`decisions/resolved/aann-behavioral-operationalization`](decisions/resolved/aann-behavioral-operationalization.md)), the v2 design frozen ([`experiments/designs/aann-construction-v2.md`](../experiments/designs/aann-construction-v2.md)), and the probe run the same session → [`result/aann-behavioral-gradient-v2`](findings/results/aann-behavioral-gradient-v2.md): all 3 models track the human Exp-2 gradient (ρ 0.68–0.75) and replicate it on frequency-matched held-out adjectives. **Inferential half tested (2026-06-13): v3 a ceiling-bounded NULL → v4 PARTIAL.** v3 ([`result/aann-inferential-v3`](findings/results/aann-inferential-v3.md)) could not measure a shift — the plural control already carried the unification reading. v4 ([`result/aann-inferential-v4`](findings/results/aann-inferential-v4.md), fifth session) removed that ceiling with a **distributive-default control**: all three models then shift paraphrase selection toward unification (Δ² +0.78/+0.70/+0.96, net of a lexical-cue control), but the shift converges across instruments (paraphrase + NLI + agreement reflex) in **only one model** (gpt-5.4-mini); claude + gemini stay paraphrase-only → **PARTIAL**. So the inferential clause moves from "untestable at this instrument" to **partially supported** — not established across the panel. **Agreement reflex generalized (2026-06-14):** [`result/aann-agreement-reflex-v5`](findings/results/aann-agreement-reflex-v5.md) re-ran the was/were agreement arm on fresh held-out items → REFLEX-GENERALIZES-TO-PANEL (gpt replicates +0.43; claude off-ceiling +0.33, temporal-subset-driven; gemini at ceiling) — a *form/agreement*-rung generalization, not an inference upgrade)
- [`findings/conjectures/way-construction.md`](findings/conjectures/way-construction.md) — status: **tested** (2026-05-29); path-traversal (self-motion) inference from non-motion verbs. **Probed this session** → [`result/way-construction-traversal-v1`](findings/results/way-construction-traversal-v1.md): confirmed above the ratified bar (way 77.8–100%, gap 77.7–100 pp, 3/3 models, both instruments; anti-motion guard holds; idiomatic guard 0%). gpt-5.4-mini the conservative outlier (4–5 scattered non-affirms). Anchored to the Scivetti way-manner subset (`way-construction-anchor`, ratified).
- [`findings/conjectures/function-word-substitutability.md`](findings/conjectures/function-word-substitutability.md) — status: **`tested` — build-v2 RUN, CONFIRM 3/3 (non-uniform)** (2026-06-21, session 69; build v1 NO-GO sessions 67–68). Function-word swaps predicted to flip an inference more than a frequency+length-matched content-word swap. Build-v1 NO-GO (~66 items, 3 classes, freq residual — [`result/function-word-swap-build-v1`](findings/results/function-word-swap-build-v1.md)); the count-vs-matching tension was **resolved** [`decisions/resolved/function-word-count-vs-matching`](decisions/resolved/function-word-count-vs-matching.md) (widen the inventory, length stays a hard gate). **Build-v2** (206 matched items, 4 classes, arms because/some/will/few; two fresh pre-run critics: NO-GO→fixed→GO; $0.502; post-run-verifier-reproduced) **CONFIRMS in all 3 models** — function-word swaps flip 3-way NLI far more than matched content swaps (content flip 1–4%, falsify arm un-fired) — **but non-uniformly**: strong & panel-consistent for `because`→`although` and `some`→`every`, **near-null for `will`→`would`** (all models), and `few`→`many` **splits the panel** (claude +0.095 vs gpt/gemini +0.96; few is 61% of items so it dominates the pooled magnitude). Prediction 3 holds at the content-class level, not the function-type level. Result: [`result/function-word-swap-run-v2`](findings/results/function-word-swap-run-v2.md). Yardstick: [`decisions/resolved/function-word-anchor-design`](decisions/resolved/function-word-anchor-design.md); norm [`resource/subtlex-us-frequency`](base/resources/subtlex-us-frequency.md). (**grammatical/lexical track**)
- [`findings/conjectures/caused-motion-construction.md`](findings/conjectures/caused-motion-construction.md) — status: **tested** (2026-05-29); transitive causation-of-motion from non-motion verbs. **Probed this session** → [`result/caused-motion-minimal-pair-divergence-v1`](findings/results/caused-motion-minimal-pair-divergence-v1.md): confirmed **at ceiling** (cm 90–100%, gap 70–100 pp, 3/3 models, atypical-robust; causation-specific control passed). Lead caveat: ceiling on easy controls. Anchored to the Scivetti caused-motion subset (`caused-motion-anchor`, ratified).
- [`findings/conjectures/conative-construction.md`](findings/conjectures/conative-construction.md) — status: **tested** (2026-05-29); cancellation of the completed-contact entailment (verb held constant). **Probed this session** → [`result/conative-minimal-pair-divergence-v1`](findings/results/conative-minimal-pair-divergence-v1.md): P1 confirmed at the ratified bar (forced-choice gap 42–88 pp 3/3 models; NLI 54–67 pp 2/3), P2/P3 supported; standing caveat = gpt-5.4-mini fails under NLI but recovers under forced-choice. Anchored to the Scivetti conative subset (`conative-anchor`, ratified).
- [`findings/conjectures/comparative-correlative-construction.md`](findings/conjectures/comparative-correlative-construction.md) — status: **tested** (2026-05-29); decoder LLMs use the CC's proportional-covariation meaning. **Probed this session** → [`result/comparative-correlative-covariation-v1`](findings/results/comparative-correlative-covariation-v1.md): the "use" core is supported at ceiling; the "narrows-but-not-closes" clause is *not* supported by the v1 instrument (panel matched the human baseline). Anchored to the Scivetti CC subset (`comparative-correlative-anchor`, ratified).
- [`findings/conjectures/lexical-sense-gradience.md`](findings/conjectures/lexical-sense-gradience.md) — status: **tested; clauses (a)+(c) supported (v1), (b) NOT established — a POWERED null at the WiC anchor (v3, 2026-05-31), after an untestable-at-DWUG null (v2)**. The project's **first lexical conjecture**. v1 → [`result/lexical-sense-gradience-v1`](findings/results/lexical-sense-gradience-v1.md): graded rating monotonic in the human DURel median (Spearman 0.60–0.83), survives a context-similarity control (a+c). Clause (b) discreteness ran as v2 ([`result/lexical-polysemy-homonymy-v2`](findings/results/lexical-polysemy-homonymy-v2.md): untestable at DWUG — 3 homonyms) then v3 ([`result/lexical-polysemy-homonymy-v3`](findings/results/lexical-polysemy-homonymy-v3.md): homonymy-enriched WiC noun subset → **powered null** on the separation test; the one floor-piling positive is confounded with plain graded distance, lemma-concentrated, scale-quirk-amplified, CI-fragile). So the distinctive discrete-regime bet (b) is **not established**; the central bet (a+c) stands. Anchored to [`resource/dwug-usage-graphs`](base/resources/dwug-usage-graphs.md) (a+c) + [`resource/wic-word-in-context`](base/resources/wic-word-in-context.md) (b). `contingent-on: []`.

- [`findings/conjectures/multimodal-lexical-grounding-divergence.md`](findings/conjectures/multimodal-lexical-grounding-divergence.md) — status: **proposed** (2026-05-30); the project's **first multimodal conjecture and first `grounded`-tagged finding** (the `grounded.perceptual` tag's first empirical exercise). Directional claim: a VLM *given disambiguating images* produces graded sense-relatedness behavior **closer to the human DURel signal** than the same family's *text-only* behavior — concentrated where senses are **perceptually distinguishable** — beyond what the text distribution already supplies; the **text-only baseline is the null to beat**, with a *redundancy null* ("text already had it") and a *distraction null* both first-class. Extends [`conjecture/lexical-sense-gradience`](findings/conjectures/lexical-sense-gradience.md) by toggling one factor (modality); offers a **second route to clause (b)** (polysemy/homonymy) the text-only [`result/lexical-polysemy-homonymy-v2`](findings/results/lexical-polysemy-homonymy-v2.md) null could not reach. Prediction 1 (Lancaster-norms moderation of the existing lexical result) **TESTED 2026-05-30 ($0) → a NULL** ([`result/lexical-perceptual-grounding-moderation-v1`](findings/results/lexical-perceptual-grounding-moderation-v1.md)): a word's perceptual groundedness does not predict text-only sense-tracking quality (underpowered; lowers the prior on the image predictions 2–4 without falsifying them). Image predictions 2–3 have since **RUN (2026-05-31) → a redundancy NULL** ([`result/multimodal-grounding-image-v1`](findings/results/multimodal-grounding-image-v1.md)): showing the picture does not improve homonym sense-separation because the text-only panel already separates perfectly. `anchor: pending` for further image predictions; panel/theory/anchor-class **ratified** (Q3=B GO, 2026-05-31) and the image anchor ratified → `contingent-on: []`. (**multimodal axis**)
- [`findings/conjectures/constructional-monotonicity-asymmetry.md`](findings/conjectures/constructional-monotonicity-asymmetry.md) — status: proposed (2026-05-31); **the project's own ORIGINAL conjecture**, abstracting the recurring add/cancel pattern across the argument-structure results into a **monotonicity asymmetry**: current decoders readily *license* a construction-contributed (added) inference but resist *suppressing* a lexically-default one — better at monotone accumulation than at defeasance. De-confounded from ceiling by [`result/conative-cancel-direction-v2`](findings/results/conative-cancel-direction-v2.md) (about direction, not ceiling); both directions bounded ([`result/coercion-implicit-cue-v2b`](findings/results/coercion-implicit-cue-v2b.md)). Mechanism labeled speculation (distributional-prior-compatible). Sharp confirm/falsify (matched-difficulty generalization to new add/cancel pairs; cancel more instrument-fragile). Candidate anchor Scivetti CxNLI. `contingent-on: []`. (**theory session**)
- [`findings/conjectures/distributional-saturation-grounding-headroom.md`](findings/conjectures/distributional-saturation-grounding-headroom.md) — status: proposed (2026-05-31); **the project's own ORIGINAL conjecture**, generalizing the two grounding nulls into one structural principle — the **grounding-headroom hypothesis**: perceptual input can move an LLM's lexical-sense behavior **only in the residual the text distribution under-determines**, and for concrete sense that residual is empirically narrow (text saturates clear homonyms → the redundancy null). `refines` [`conjecture/multimodal-lexical-grounding-divergence`](findings/conjectures/multimodal-lexical-grounding-divergence.md) by adding the positive *where*-to-look coordinate (the under-determination residual, not merely "visually distinguishable"). Sharp confirm/falsify (image helps in the AUC<1.0 residual, null at saturation; negative separability×improvement correlation; distraction-controlled). Candidate next task VWSD. `contingent-on: []`. (**theory session / multimodal axis**)
- [`findings/conjectures/commutative-convention.md`](findings/conjectures/commutative-convention.md) — status: **RETIRED — FALSIFIED (2026-06-16, twentieth session)** by [`result/relational-spontaneous-recency-a`](findings/results/relational-spontaneous-recency-a.md) (Option A): when a term is **reassigned** so only recency disambiguates, both models recover it by its **most-recent binding** at ceiling → **order-sensitive (non-commutative)**. The positive is promoted to [`claim/relational-order-sensitive-reassignment`](findings/claims/relational-order-sensitive-reassignment.md); commutativity is **operationalization-dependent** (the v1/v4 nulls stand as bounded observations where order carried no disambiguating signal or was confounded with position). *Original (proposed, 2026-05-31):* **the project's own ORIGINAL conjecture**, naming the relational pilot's verdict precisely: LLM referential conventions are (so far) **commutative** — recovered from the content-*set*, not the ordered trajectory — the **aggregation (commutative) vs. constitution (non-commutative)** distinction that makes "coordination, not constitution" exact. A deflationary forward bet that the order-invariance persists; the predicted human contrast was sharpened 2026-06-12 against [`base/sources/brennan-clark-1996-conceptual-pacts.md`](base/sources/brennan-clark-1996-conceptual-pacts.md): humans form partner-indexed, historical pacts (anchored), while human *order-sensitivity* — the pole the contrast needs — is untested by that source (it reports frequency-over-recency) and stays an open question. Decisive test = the v2 history-perturbation arm — **first attempt ran 2026-06-12 → INCONCLUSIVE/MIXED** ([`result/relational-history-perturbation-v2`](findings/results/relational-history-perturbation-v2.md)): neither falsified nor strengthened; the test remains open (position/chronology confound identified by the direction-control arm). Generalizes a bounded, under-powered null ([`result/relational-reference-game-v1`](findings/results/relational-reference-game-v1.md)); trajectory measure internal-contrast-only; v1 yardstick **ratified 2026-06-12**. `contingent-on: []`. (**theory session / relational axis**)
- [`findings/conjectures/preference-commitment-generality.md`](findings/conjectures/preference-commitment-generality.md) — status: **tested → NOT CONFIRMED** (2026-06-15); the forward bet that the AANN preference/commitment dissociation is a **general property of divergent-default constructions** was tested on the conative ([`result/conative-preference-commitment-v1`](findings/results/conative-preference-commitment-v1.md), VERDICT INCONCLUSIVE) and the **first generalization attempt failed to reproduce the AANN shape**: the paraphrase double contrast was non-positive in all three models (the bare-*at* lexical cue absorbs the cancel-preference) and the only construction effect was a single model's *commitment-only* shift — the mirror of AANN. The dissociation reads as **AANN-specific so far**; the conceptual "two constructs" point survives, the "general ordering" claim does not. One construction cannot prove AANN-uniqueness — the way/caused-motion near-miss fallback could revisit it. `contingent-on: []`. (**grammatical / empirical track**)

### Findings — essays

- [`findings/essays/cross-level-convergence-ladder.md`](findings/essays/cross-level-convergence-ladder.md) — status: **revised** (2026-06-22; **trigger (b) FIRED session 84** — the cross-level shape dissolved at R2 in [`result/cross-level-shared-instrument-v1`](findings/results/cross-level-shared-instrument-v1.md), the anticipated worked example of a rhyme correctly *not* promoted to a mechanism); "**From rhyme to mechanism**" — a reusable **evidence standard** (a graded *convergence ladder*: **R0** shared vocabulary → **R1** native-instrument agreement → **R2** instrument-equalized → **R3** break-test survival → **R-ceiling** mechanistic identity, named out-of-reach for a behavioral project) for when a cross-level / cross-instrument **family resemblance** may be upgraded to a **single-mechanism** claim. The rule: assert a cross-level unification **only at the rung the evidence has reached**; below R2 it stays a *rhyme*, filed as an open-question, never a finding. The **symmetric twin** of [`essay/undischargeable-negative`](findings/essays/undischargeable-negative.md) (you can't prove "one mechanism" from rhyme, as you can't prove "M cannot" from behavior); break-test logic from [`essay/output-channel-confound`](findings/essays/output-channel-confound.md); explicitly **distinct** from the construction evidence-ladder (one-mechanism-vs-rhyme, not meaning-vs-form). `refines` the OQ; `supports` [`conjecture/cross-level-gradience-aggregate-not-moment`](findings/conjectures/cross-level-gradience-aggregate-not-moment.md). (created 2026-06-22; **method essay**)
- [`findings/essays/ambiguity-kind-not-level.md`](findings/essays/ambiguity-kind-not-level.md) — status: **revised** (2026-06-23, session 87 — **trigger (b) FIRED: the central reading DISSOLVED at R2 for the lexical case**, [`result/within-lexical-scalar-vs-disjunctive-v1`](findings/results/within-lexical-scalar-vs-disjunctive-v1.md) returned **SURVIVAL 3/3** — the models commit on a balanced homonym too, so the lexical specialness is the **word-sense layer, not the scalar-vs-disjunctive kind**; the kind-reading is retracted for the lexical case [kept visible], the conceptual scalar/disjunctive contrast survives, one residual bounds "layer" [a balanced homonym is still resolvable-by-committing]); originally **draft** (2026-06-22, session 85); **"Kind, not level"** — a **re-reading** of the cross-level dissolution ([`result/cross-level-shared-instrument-v1`](findings/results/cross-level-shared-instrument-v1.md)). Argues the dissolution's commit/decline split is more parsimoniously indexed by the **kind** of indeterminacy than by the **level**: the models *commit* on a **scalar** ambiguity (a graded similarity with a *nearer pole* to lean to — the lexical bridging stimulus) and *decline* on a **disjunctive** one (two complete readings/bindings, *both/neither*, no nearer pole — the constructional/relational items), so the lexical leg's specialness may be the **softness of its stimulus, not the word-sense layer**. Explicitly **does NOT revive** the dissolved level-conjecture: kind is confounded with level in that design, so the kind-reading is held at **R1** on the [`convergence ladder`](findings/essays/cross-level-convergence-ladder.md), *not* asserted as a finding, and routed to the matched-ambiguity-kind probe ([`decisions/resolved/matched-ambiguity-kind-cross-level`](decisions/resolved/matched-ambiguity-kind-cross-level.md), **ratified session 86 → the within-lexical probe is now buildable**). The discriminating test: a *disjunctively*-ambiguous lexical item (balanced homonym, no tie-break) should draw decline, not commitment, if kind (not layer) drives the split. `refines` the OQ; `depends-on` the result, the dissolved conjecture, the ladder, the three level-home essays, [`concept/polysemy`](base/concepts/polysemy.md) + [`concept/distributional-meaning`](base/concepts/distributional-meaning.md). **No new empirical claim; no human comparison.** (created 2026-06-22; **philosophical track**)
- [`findings/essays/layer-specialness-vs-always-resolvability.md`](findings/essays/layer-specialness-vs-always-resolvability.md) — status: **revised** (2026-06-23, session 91 — **trigger (c) FIRED**: the discriminating probe was *attempted* under the resolved gate and **terminated at certification** — Q1-ii, the independent not-model-based balance check, is not satisfiable under no-human-subjects; fork **stays at R1**, no model run, $0 → [`result/forced-both-lexical-build-attempt-v1`](findings/results/forced-both-lexical-build-attempt-v1.md), VERDICT-SOUND on independent review); originally **draft** (2026-06-23, session 88); the successor to (and `refines`) [`essay/ambiguity-kind-not-level`](findings/essays/ambiguity-kind-not-level.md), written the same session 87's SURVIVAL result landed it. Takes the **load-bearing residual (caveat 1)** of [`result/within-lexical-scalar-vs-disjunctive-v1`](findings/results/within-lexical-scalar-vs-disjunctive-v1.md) and forks the *surviving* lexical commit into two rival readings: **(A) layer-specialness** (the word-sense layer always draws a discrete pick, whatever the kind/structure of ambiguity) vs **(B) always-resolvability** (the models commit wherever a reading is *pickable*, and word-sense has only ever presented pickable items — so the lexical leg looks special only because its ambiguities stay resolvable). Shows the SURVIVAL design **cannot separate** them (a balanced homonym is *both* lexical *and* resolvable, so both readings predict commit), and names the one stimulus that would — a **genuinely-unresolvable lexical item** (a forced-both pun / zeugma, the lexical analogue of the relational same-round **dual binding**), with the **asymmetric prediction**: commit under (A), decline under (B). Leads with the honest certification difficulty (the "it means both" third response makes the verdict an artifact of the scoring rule unless the instrument asks a *forced-single-application* question). Bridges to [`essay/transcript-ceiling`](findings/essays/transcript-ceiling.md)'s **single-reader-recoverability** criterion (reading (B) = lexical ambiguities stay on the *thin/recoverable* side; the bridge is the *criterion*, not the constitution metaphysics) and to [`concept/distributional-meaning`](base/concepts/distributional-meaning.md) (B predicts a lexical genuine-both with no distributional tie-break draws **abstention**). Held at **R1** on the [`convergence ladder`](findings/essays/cross-level-convergence-ladder.md), with the **deflationary (B) holding the burden**. `refines` [`essay/ambiguity-kind-not-level`](findings/essays/ambiguity-kind-not-level.md) + [`essay/graded-scale-ungraded-commitment`](findings/essays/graded-scale-ungraded-commitment.md); `depends-on` the two results, the ladder, transcript-ceiling, [`concept/polysemy`](base/concepts/polysemy.md) + [`concept/distributional-meaning`](base/concepts/distributional-meaning.md). **No new empirical claim; no human comparison; the discriminating probe has not run.** The R2-rung operationalization the essay named — how to build + score a forced-both lexical item — was **ratified session 90 (2026-06-23, ADOPT DEFAULTS)**: [`decisions/resolved/forced-both-lexical-operationalization`](decisions/resolved/forced-both-lexical-operationalization.md), so a forced-both probe is now **buildable under the resolved gate + a fresh pre-run critic** (the essay stays at R1, unaffected; trigger (c) "cannot cleanly certify" the honest expected first outcome). (created 2026-06-23; **lexical / philosophical track**)
- [`findings/essays/aggregation-not-constitution.md`](findings/essays/aggregation-not-constitution.md) — status: **revised** (2026-06-12 trigger c-ii; **2026-06-16 trigger (a) fired**); **the project's FIRST essay** (the philosophical track's first-class artifact). Argues that the relational pilot's "coordination, not constitution" null, made precise by the commutative/non-commutative distinction, deflates exactly one thing — the empirical shortcut from observed convergent convention-use between LLMs (Ashery's naming games, Imai's reference games, the project's own pilot) to meaning constituted *between* them — because none of those designs detects the non-commutative surplus constitution would require. It does **not** touch Brandom's normative inferentialism (deontic scorekeeping was never measured) or any metaphysical thesis (a bounded under-powered null cannot reach one). The conceptual-pact paragraph was rewritten 2026-06-12 against the now-in-repo [`base/sources/brennan-clark-1996-conceptual-pacts.md`](base/sources/brennan-clark-1996-conceptual-pacts.md). **2026-06-16:** the decisive v5/Option-A history-perturbation arm fired trigger (a) — the *commutativity* sub-claim is **falsified where order disambiguates** ([`result/relational-spontaneous-recency-a`](findings/results/relational-spontaneous-recency-a.md); conjecture retired). The deflationary leg is **half-overturned per the essay's own spec**: the convention is now **order-sensitive but thin** (latest-binding-wins), still **not constituted-between**; the anti-Brandomian friction reverses *in direction only, at the commutativity grain* (the gap to deontic scorekeeping untouched); the "convergence is the floor" method and all of "What the null does not touch" survive intact. **2026-06-17:** the implicit-reassignment control ([`result/relational-implicit-reassignment-control`](findings/results/relational-implicit-reassignment-control.md)) strengthened (did not overturn) the Option-A positive — bound (2) tightened to *flag-not-directed*, the third deflation's reversal made sturdier-not-larger; still thin latest-binding-wins, still not constitution. **2026-06-17 (later session):** the rung-(ii) integration result ([`result/relational-integration-rung-ii`](findings/results/relational-integration-rung-ii.md)) was folded in — a *compatible* earlier turn **survives** and the two **compose**, so the update rule is enriched to **supersede-on-conflict, compose-on-compatibility**; the deflationary leg gains a second thin-side instance (composition is single-reader-recoverable) and nothing in "What the null does not touch" moves; still not constitution. (**relational axis / philosophical track**)
- [`findings/essays/conversation-as-text-not-timeline.md`](findings/essays/conversation-as-text-not-timeline.md) — status: **revised** (2026-06-14 draft; **2026-06-16 triggers (a)+(b) fired → thesis scoped**); **the project's FOURTH essay** (relational / philosophical track), the successor to (and `refines`) the first. It argued, from the **history-perturbation v4** within-arm decoupling, that to these models a conversation is **prose geometry — a layout, not a timeline** (under conflict both models anchored on physical text position, not chronology). **2026-06-16:** both its revision triggers fired — the Option-B stamp-comprehension gate ([`result/relational-stamp-comprehension-b`](findings/results/relational-stamp-comprehension-b.md), both models read the stamp on demand) and the Option-A arm ([`result/relational-spontaneous-recency-a`](findings/results/relational-spontaneous-recency-a.md), both track stamped recency at ceiling once position is neutralized and order is the sole disambiguator). The "layout, full stop" thesis is therefore **scoped, not deleted** (over-general framings kept visible with in-place SCOPED notes): the picture is now **regime-dependent** — the surface cue (last-on-page) governs when available and sufficient (v4), but the models **recover and use stamped recency when it is the only disambiguator** (Option A). The methodological **located-confound** lesson survives and is *strengthened* (Option A is the decoupled design the v4 sting demanded). Stale caveats fixed: stamp-blindness **resolved** (Option B), the conjecture **retired/falsified** (Option A). Bounds: thin-not-rich; spontaneous≠cue-free; `internal-contrast-only`; v1/v4 nulls **bounded, not overturned**. **2026-06-17:** the implicit-reassignment control strengthened the Option-A regime's recency-tracking (bound (2) tightened to *flag-not-directed*); scoped conclusion unchanged. **2026-06-17 (later session):** the rung-(ii) integration result ([`result/relational-integration-rung-ii`](findings/results/relational-integration-rung-ii.md)) adds a **third regime** — when two turns are *compatible*, both models **compose** them (answer = the conjunction; physical position again at chance) — confirming the regime-dependent reading ("a layout, full stop" is false in general; the governing cue is whichever one the task makes load-bearing: text position in v4, stamped recency in Option A, the conjunction here). Still thin, still `internal-contrast-only`. (**relational axis / philosophical track**)
- [`findings/essays/preference-without-commitment.md`](findings/essays/preference-without-commitment.md) — status: **revised** (2026-06-14; draft→revised when the v6 replication landed); **the project's THIRD essay** (grammatical / philosophical track). Argues, from the AANN inferential **v4 PARTIAL — now replicated cell-for-cell by [`result/aann-inferential-v6`](findings/results/aann-inferential-v6.md) across two disjoint item sets** — that a forced-choice paraphrase *preference* and an NLI entailment *commitment* are evidence for **two different constructs** — graded **distributional compatibility** (a use/family-resemblance probe) vs. defeasible **inferential commitment** (a truth-conditional / inferentialist probe) — **not** two noisy readings of one latent "use." Where they dissociate (v4/v6: the construction shifts paraphrase preference in all three models but carries to NLI + the agreement reflex in only gpt-5.4-mini — the "largest forced-choice-vs-NLI disagreement in the project's record", and **off-ceiling**, so genuine divergence not compression), "does the model *use* the construction's meaning?" has **no single model-level answer**: "use" decomposes into a preference component (present panel-wide) and a commitment component (present in one model). Maps FC→Wittgensteinian use-pole, NLI→truth-conditional pole — the two semantic theories pulling apart inside one model's behavior — and draws the consequence that the evidence ladder's **top two rungs can come apart**, which v4/v6 instance. Companion to (and `refines`) the second essay: that one is about the question being *unreachable* (v3 ceiling); this one about it being *reachable but the instruments disagreeing*. `internal-contrast-only`; explicit revision triggers — **(a) powered NLI convergence for claude/gemini → retract for them, and (b) FC shift failing to replicate → thesis weakens were both EXERCISED by v6 and NEITHER fired** (claude/gemini NLI still did not converge; the FC shift did replicate), so the essay was *strengthened*, not retracted; a human anchor entering would still revisit the caveat. **2026-06-15 scope-limiting datum (no trigger fired):** the first attempt to generalize the dissociation to a different construction came back negative ([`result/conative-preference-commitment-v1`](findings/results/conative-preference-commitment-v1.md), INCONCLUSIVE) — bounding the essay's instanced scope to AANN (the two-constructs *type* point stands; any *general-ordering* reading is contradicted by data). (**grammatical / philosophical track**)
- [`findings/essays/inference-default-coincidence.md`](findings/essays/inference-default-coincidence.md) — status: **draft** (2026-06-13); **the project's SECOND essay** (grammatical / philosophical track). Argues one bounded *methodological* thesis from the AANN inferential v3 ceiling-bounded null: for a next-token model, a construction's **licensed inference can be behaviorally indistinguishable from the phrase's distributional default**, and where the two **coincide** a shift-from-control design cannot reach the inferential question at all — "the default eats the construction." Names the **two compounding limits** (can't-say-like-humans = `internal-contrast-only`; can't-separate-from-the-default = the coincidence) and draws the evidence-ladder consequence: the top rung (inferential *use*) may be **unreachable by within-model contrast for exactly the constructions whose contributed reading is most entrenched as a default** — a selection effect, not a verdict on the models. Joins this to the lexicon–grammar continuum as the **grammatical-side analogue** of the lexical/multimodal saturation (text already carries the distinction). The lone v3 positive — gpt-5.4-mini's singular-agreement reflex — sharpens, not undercuts, the thesis (it moved precisely where the default points the *other* way). Explicit revision triggers (a v4 distributive-default control that *does* register a shift; a human AANN-inference dataset; a clean Option-B divergence result; representational evidence). Rests entirely on the `internal-contrast-only` v3 result; no human-comparison claim, no resource anchor owed. (**grammatical / philosophical track**)
- [`findings/essays/inherited-not-constituted.md`](findings/essays/inherited-not-constituted.md) — status: **draft** (2026-06-14); **the project's FIFTH essay** (philosophical track), a cross-source synthesis bridging [`base/sources/grindrod-2024-linguistic-intentionality.md`](base/sources/grindrod-2024-linguistic-intentionality.md) to the project's own [`findings/essays/aggregation-not-constitution.md`](findings/essays/aggregation-not-constitution.md). Argues the two draw **one line from opposite directions**: Grindrod argues *metasemantically* that LLM outputs are meaningful because **linguistic** intentionality depends on a pre-existing **public language the model inherits** (Evans/Millikan), and the project argues *behaviorally* (the relational null) that apparent between-agent meaning is **aggregation, not constitution** — both locating content in something **prior and public**, neither in the model's originating act nor the live exchange. A prominent **"The gap" section** holds the discipline: this is a convergence of *picture, not a shared proof* — the behavioral null does **not** confirm Grindrod's metasemantics and vice versa; the strongest relation asserted is an **expectation-match** (the bounded null is what one would expect if content is inherited-and-public). No new empirical claim. Revision triggers: a future relational experiment showing non-commutative constitution weakens the behavioral leg; cataloguing a Grindrod rebuttal re-weights the metasemantic leg. (**philosophical track**)
- [`findings/essays/reference-as-premise-bound.md`](findings/essays/reference-as-premise-bound.md) — status: **revised** (2026-06-15, triggers (d)+(e) fired); **the project's SIXTH essay** (referential / philosophical track). Argues the in-repo dispute over whether an LLM's words **refer** (word-to-world) is **premise-bound, not evidence-bound**: [`base/sources/mandelkern-linzen-2024-do-words-refer.md`](base/sources/mandelkern-linzen-2024-do-words-refer.md) and the project's own [`base/concepts/referential-meaning.md`](base/concepts/referential-meaning.md) run the **same** externalist (Putnam/Kripke) metasemantics to **opposite** verdicts, disagreeing only on the antecedent of M&L's §4.3 community-membership conditional ("*If* they are part of a linguistic community … then their use … refers") — a fact fixed **off-board** (by natural history, not any in-head/in-behavior fact), so **no behavioral probe the project can run adjudicates it**. The original contribution is the **structural diagnosis**: this is a cell of the meaning map where the project's behavioral method is *constitutively* silent — a principled limit, not a gap more probes can close. Draws **two citation-discipline consequences**: (1) don't cite the grounding nulls as bearing against reference (history-channel vs perception-channel orthogonality); (2) don't cite M&L as *establishing* reference (its verdict is modal/premise-conditional) — cite it only as making the concept page's in-principle "no" *contestable*. Stays descriptivist; ranks neither pole. Distinct from the relational essays (word-to-world axis + a premise *no probe reaches*, vs. the relational axis + a *null a probe produced*). Revision triggers: a probe that genuinely bears on word-to-world reference; a human reference-anchor entering the repo; the Putnam/Evans/Kripke primaries entering; a published M&L rebuttal catalogued. **Revised 2026-06-15:** triggers (d) and (e) fired together — the pro-reference pole, "uncontested in-repo" only one session earlier, is now contested by **two** published replies: the internalist [`base/sources/baggio-murphy-2024-internalist-rejoinder.md`](base/sources/baggio-murphy-2024-internalist-rejoinder.md) (denies the §4.3 antecedent *and* rejects the externalist frame) and the intramural-externalist [`base/sources/ostertag-2025-externalist-reply.md`](base/sources/ostertag-2025-externalist-reply.md) (the naïve-natural-history route fails on its own terms). The central thesis is **unchanged and better-instanced**: all three published parties argue by *conceptual* means and **none adduces a measurement**, which is premise-bound-not-evidence-bound exhibited by the disputants' own practice — Ostertag even frames his disagreement as turning on an antecedent he doubts, not the conditional he accepts. New trigger (f): a published voice claiming a *measurement* settles LM reference would directly challenge the thesis. (**referential / philosophical track**)
- [`findings/essays/reference-denials-disunified.md`](findings/essays/reference-denials-disunified.md) — status: **draft** (2026-06-16); **the project's SEVENTH essay** (referential / philosophical track), the sibling of (and complement to) the sixth. Where the sixth anatomizes the *yes-vs-no* disagreement, this one anatomizes the **internal disunity of the "no" camp**: the repo now holds **three structurally distinct denials** of LM reference — signal-based ([`base/sources/bender-koller-2020-climbing.md`](base/sources/bender-koller-2020-climbing.md)), internalist frame-rejection ([`base/sources/baggio-murphy-2024-internalist-rejoinder.md`](base/sources/baggio-murphy-2024-internalist-rejoinder.md) §4), and externalist-membership ([`base/concepts/referential-meaning.md`](base/concepts/referential-meaning.md); Baggio & Murphy §5; the §4/§5 incompatibility is *intra-paper*) — plus Ostertag as an open-verdict route-critic. They share today's verdict but give **incompatible counterfactuals** for what would lift it (a missing *signal*; a missing *social-historical status*; a missing *mind* — and internalism says no built world-relation suffices). The original contribution is this **counterfactual-divergence diagnosis**: the referential "no" is not one boundary but several that coincide on current models. Draws **two page-corrections**: (1) the deflationary concept page must record the denial as a *family*, not anchor it to one argument; (2) [`findings/theory/situating-llm-meaning.md`](findings/theory/situating-llm-meaning.md)'s "only a built world-relation moves the referential cell" prediction is **frame-relative** (false on internalism). `refines` both corrected pages; `depends-on` the sixth essay. No new empirical claim; every quote cites its in-repo page. Revision triggers: a unifying meta-theory of the denials; a reference-specific signal-based denial superseding B&K; the externalist primaries entering; a probe bearing on word-to-world reference; a published voice arguing the denials *converge*. (**referential / philosophical track**)
- [`findings/essays/update-is-not-constitution.md`](findings/essays/update-is-not-constitution.md) — status: **revised** (2026-06-17 draft; **2026-06-17 trigger (a) fired → rung (ii) occupied**; **2026-06-18** Option-C made composition order-sensitive, occupied by claude only under a forced format + rung (iii) rich side documented structurally closed for text; **2026-06-19** the stricter thin rung is now **panel-concordant given a working surface** across two non-commuting pairs [D4, A4] — superseding the one-model reading as a forced-format/output-channel artifact, still THIN); **the project's EIGHTH essay** (relational / philosophical track), built on the "order-sensitive but thin" relational positive ([`claim/relational-order-sensitive-reassignment`](findings/claims/relational-order-sensitive-reassignment.md)). Its contribution is **conceptual, not empirical**: it builds the structure [`concept/relational-meaning`](base/concepts/relational-meaning.md) said was missing — a **four-rung ladder** above the relational bottom ((i) order-sensitive *overwrite* = latest-binding-wins; (ii) order-sensitive *integration* / non-overwrite repair; (iii) *path-dependence* proper / live-vs-shuffled; (iv) genuine *between-agent constitution* / Brandomian scorekeeping), each with a candidate behavioral signature and a discriminating design — plus a sharp **single-reader-recoverability criterion** cutting thin (updated) from rich (constituted): a convention is *thin* if its recovered interpretation is computable by any single reader from the record's content+stamps, *rich* only if recovery requires a surplus no single reader could reconstruct. Argues "**updating a convention is not constituting one**". **2026-06-17: rung (ii) now OCCUPIED** ([`result/relational-integration-rung-ii`](findings/results/relational-integration-rung-ii.md)) — both models compose a compatible earlier turn at ceiling (overwrite rate 0.000), so the rule is **supersede-on-conflict, compose-on-compatibility**; **but both occupied rungs (i),(ii) sit on the THIN side**, and the result shows *survival* not order-sensitive composition (symmetric design) and is only weak evidence of *spontaneous* composition (trivially-easy conjunction). Rungs (iii)–(iv) stay *unbuilt*; the instrument **cannot separate rung (i)/(ii) from (iii)** (the claim's scope limit 3); the firm thin floor makes the *distance* to constitution measurable and large. **No human comparison** (cited results `internal-contrast-only`). Remaining triggers: a live-vs-shuffled (rung iii) separation; a between-agent scorekeeping observable (rung iv); a human order/path anchor; or a result showing the rung-(ii) composition is itself *order-sensitive*. `refines` [`concept/relational-meaning`](base/concepts/relational-meaning.md) + [`essay/aggregation-not-constitution`](findings/essays/aggregation-not-constitution.md); `contingent-on: []`. (**relational axis / philosophical track**)
- [`findings/essays/transcript-ceiling.md`](findings/essays/transcript-ceiling.md) — status: **live** (2026-06-17 draft; **promoted to live 2026-06-18** — its named puncture test, revision trigger (a), was run in a *later* session ([`result/relational-order-composition-c`](findings/results/relational-order-composition-c.md), the strongest order-load-bearing text design buildable) and did **not** fire: the pre-run gate ruled the operation-order gap THIN, corroborating the ceiling. `live` = an active standing position, **not** proven; all four triggers stay live, (a) for *other* Option-C designs); **the project's NINTH essay** (relational / philosophical track), the cross-cutting successor to (and `refines`) the eighth. Asks whether the project's recurring **single-reader-recoverability** criterion — the [`essay/update-is-not-constitution`](findings/essays/update-is-not-constitution.md) thin/rich cut — is a fact about *these models* or about *the text medium they are probed in*. Defends, as a **conjecture about the project's own method** (hedged throughout, not a proof): the cut tracks the **record itself**, so a text-only probe is **structurally ceilinged at the thin side** — it can show updating, integration, even non-commuting operations, but the rich-side surplus (a live two-party normative trajectory; arrival-order not encoded in the final state) is constitutively *not in any transcript*. Argument in three steps: the rich side is *defined* by what the record lacks; a transcript states a record and nothing more; therefore the probe's reachable space is the thin side entire. Adopts (does not deny) the just-ratified rung-(iii) **Option-C escape hatch** — an operation-order gap *might* puncture the ceiling, which is exactly the decision's pre-run-adjudicated test — so the thesis is **falsifiable** (revision trigger (a)). The decision's own "structural-closure is a fully promotable outcome" language is the thesis arrived at independently by the adversarial reviewer. Disciplines: bounds the **medium, not the models**; the grounding nulls are flagged as a **contrast, not a confirmation** (the image null was a *redundancy* null — text carried *more*, not less); **`internal-contrast-only`, no human comparison**. `refines` [`essay/update-is-not-constitution`](findings/essays/update-is-not-constitution.md) + [`concept/relational-meaning`](base/concepts/relational-meaning.md); `contingent-on: []`. (**relational axis / philosophical track**)
- [`findings/essays/rung-iv-instrument.md`](findings/essays/rung-iv-instrument.md) — status: **draft** (2026-06-18); **the project's TENTH essay** (relational / philosophical track), the **constructive complement** to the ninth ([`essay/transcript-ceiling`](findings/essays/transcript-ceiling.md)). Where the ceiling essay argues *text cannot* reach the rich side, this one asks, forward, what an instrument that *could* reach **rung (iv)** (genuine between-agent constitution) would have to be — and answers: **a scored live practice, not a transcript.** Its defining requirement is a class of observables that exist only between parties and only while the interaction is live — Brandomian deontic scorekeeping (characterized-not-read in-repo via [`concept/inferential-meaning`](base/concepts/inferential-meaning.md)): at minimum **commitment undertaken vs merely uttered** (answerability), **entitlement granted/withheld by the other party**, and **a challenge and whether it was discharged** — each a *status instituted by uptake*, hence a surplus no single reader of a record can reconstruct, so recording it requires a live two-party practice, not a depiction (extends the ceiling essay's chess-scoresheet image to "a refereed game in progress"). Holds a key **discipline: rung (iii) ≠ rung (iv)** — a non-text medium that merely carries arrival-order surplus would bound the transcript ceiling (rung iii) but is *strictly weaker* than recording normative status (rung iv). Explicitly **builds nothing, measures nothing, promises nothing**: the instrument is a requirement-specification the project may never construct (no in-repo human dyadic resource with normative observables; Clark & Wilkes-Gibbs 1986 unfetched and scoped to collaborative reference, not scorekeeping). **No human comparison**; quotes no Brandom directly. Names exactly the event the ceiling essay's revision trigger (b) anticipates. `refines` [`essay/transcript-ceiling`](findings/essays/transcript-ceiling.md) + [`essay/update-is-not-constitution`](findings/essays/update-is-not-constitution.md); `contingent-on: []`. - [`findings/essays/capability-split.md`](findings/essays/capability-split.md) — status: **draft** (2026-06-18); **the project's ELEVENTH essay** (relational / philosophical track), a **methodological** unit prompted by Option C being the **first relational rung to split the panel** ([`result/relational-order-composition-c`](findings/results/relational-order-composition-c.md): claude RESPECTS-ORDER at ceiling, gemini UNINTERPRETABLE). Its original contribution is a **reporting discipline**, not an empirical claim: a one-model (split) positive is **not** a property of "the models"/"LLMs" but a **capability split** attributable only to the model that showed it. Rungs (i)–(ii) read as "both panel models" *because the panel happened to concord* — concordance is contingent, not a safe default. A split licenses only a per-model **existential** (claude composes two non-commuting moves at ceiling, with transparent reasoning) plus a per-model **negative** — and the negative here is an **instrument-capability limit, not a clean order-blind null** (the gate "correctly refuses to read" gemini's COMP rate; gemini cannot compose even on demand, DIRECT 0.583), so it must **not** be read as "gemini lacks order-sensitive composition in general." Standing recommendation: mark every panel verdict **CONCORDANT vs SPLIT**, never average a split into a panel-level claim (the project's past findings were *already careful* — this is forward discipline, not an accusation). Logs "claude > gemini" as a **thing to watch, not a finding** (refuses the cross-task extrapolation on one probe). **No human comparison.** **Trigger (b) tested 2026-06-18 → did NOT fire (no witness):** the easier K=4 re-run ([`result/relational-order-composition-c-easier-k4`](findings/results/relational-order-composition-c-easier-k4.md)) halved the instrument and neither gemini (0.594) nor gpt (0.438) cleared the on-demand gate, so the split survives the easing — *strengthened*, not bounded to one instrument. **Tested a SECOND time (on-signature) 2026-06-18 → again no witness:** the figure-to-figure easing ([`result/relational-order-composition-c-figure-to-figure`](findings/results/relational-order-composition-c-figure-to-figure.md)) removed the position↔figure read-off and neither gemini (0.656) nor gpt (0.250) cleared the gate; the single-move signature persisted (localizing the difficulty to chaining) → **figure-to-figure discharged**, trigger (b) live only for worked-example / fewer-steps. `refines` [`essay/update-is-not-constitution`](findings/essays/update-is-not-constitution.md); `depends-on` [`result/relational-order-composition-c`](findings/results/relational-order-composition-c.md) + [`result/relational-order-composition-c-easier-k4`](findings/results/relational-order-composition-c-easier-k4.md) + [`result/relational-order-composition-c-figure-to-figure`](findings/results/relational-order-composition-c-figure-to-figure.md) + [`claim/relational-order-sensitive-reassignment`](findings/claims/relational-order-sensitive-reassignment.md); `contingent-on: []`.
