- [`findings/essays/undischargeable-negative.md`](findings/essays/undischargeable-negative.md) — status: **draft** (2026-06-18); **the project's TWELFTH essay** (methodological / philosophical track), the **generalization** of the eleventh ([`essay/capability-split`](findings/essays/capability-split.md)) and the ninth ([`essay/transcript-ceiling`](findings/essays/transcript-ceiling.md)). Gives the charter's "write the null" discipline a **logical-epistemic backbone**: a capability *positive* is a **verifiable existential** (one witness — one elicitation on which the model succeeds — discharges it) while a capability *absence* ("M cannot do X") is an **unverifiable universal over elicitations** that no finite behavioral battery reaches — the **mirror** of the Popperian law/existence asymmetry, so from behavior alone the negative is **undischargeable**. This **vindicates** the null discipline rather than threatening it: the project's nulls are not capability-absence claims but instrument-relative facts, so writing them is honest and the only error is the silent upgrade to "M cannot." Builds a **typology of negatives** — (1) **effect-null under an instrument** (relational pilot's order-insensitivity; grounding redundancy), (2) **instrument-uninterpretable** / prerequisite-gate failure (gemini/gpt UNINTERPRETABLE on Option C), (3) **structural reach-closure** (the transcript ceiling — a negative about the *instrument's reach*, not the model's capacity) — and keeps a fourth box, a behavioral **capability-absence**, deliberately empty (only a non-behavioral architectural/mechanistic proof closes it; trigger (a)). Decision-relevant payoff: re-running a failing probe is futile (another ∀-instance, never the ∀); only a **witness-seeking** probe (an easier elicitation — exactly capability-split trigger (b)) or a structural argument can change a negative's status. Generalizes capability-split's clean-null/instrument-uninterpretable mark from the split-panel case to the single-model case, and lifts transcript-ceiling's structural closure into "kind 3." **No new empirical claim; no human comparison.** `depends-on` [`essay/capability-split`](findings/essays/capability-split.md) + [`essay/transcript-ceiling`](findings/essays/transcript-ceiling.md) + [`concept/formal-vs-functional-competence`](base/concepts/formal-vs-functional-competence.md) + [`result/relational-order-composition-c`](findings/results/relational-order-composition-c.md) + [`result/relational-reference-game-v1`](findings/results/relational-reference-game-v1.md) + [`essay/rung-iv-instrument`](findings/essays/rung-iv-instrument.md); `contingent-on: []`. (**methodological / philosophical track**)
- [`findings/essays/witness-seeking-economics.md`](findings/essays/witness-seeking-economics.md) — status: **draft** (2026-06-18; **deepened 2026-06-20, session 61** — the *partial-witness* slot, below); **the project's THIRTEENTH essay** (methodological / philosophical track), the **refinement** of the twelfth ([`essay/undischargeable-negative`](findings/essays/undischargeable-negative.md)). That essay proved a **witness-seeking** probe is the *only* behavioral move that can flip a capability-negative, but left open *how much* witness-seeking is worth — and since the elicitation space is open, "seek a witness" reads as unbounded against a finite budget ($5/day). This essay supplies the missing **economics of spending**. Its load-bearing move is the distinction between **logical closure** (a claim about the model — undischargeable from behavior, fully preserved) and **practical suspension** (a claim about the *project's spending* — provisional, reopenable, asserting nothing about the model); the project never *closes* a behavioral negative, it *suspends* the witness-search. The value of the next probe ≈ expected-info × P(fires) vs cost, where expected-info decomposes into **axis novelty** (easing the same axis twice has diminishing returns; a fresh axis is informative) and **signature match** (read the failure signature, ease the *implicated* axis — a non-witness from an off-signature easing is weak evidence). The highest-value terminator is a **structural bound** (a kind-3 reach-closure argument that retires a whole class of easings at zero spend — the transcript ceiling exemplifies it). Worked instance: the K=4 non-witness eased **one, off-signature** axis (track size, while the "single-move-reader" signature implicates *chaining*), which is exactly why [`essay/capability-split`](findings/essays/capability-split.md) correctly keeps trigger (b) live and [`NEXT.md`](../NEXT.md) names a figure-to-figure / fewer-chaining-steps probe next. Adds a **witness-search suspension** reporting note (axes eased / implicated-but-un-eased / any structural bound / reopen condition), orthogonal to capability-split's CONCORDANT-SPLIT and undischargeable-negative's kind-1/2/3 marks; **never written as "M cannot."** **The named on-signature probe then ran ([`result/relational-order-composition-c-figure-to-figure`](findings/results/relational-order-composition-c-figure-to-figure.md), 2026-06-18): no witness, the single-move signature persisting even under trivial-lookup moves — corroborating the off-signature reading of K=4, and the result page now carries the predicted suspension note (suspended on the read-off axis, not closed).** **Deepened 2026-06-20 (session 61) — the PARTIAL WITNESS:** session 60's let-alone forced-decomposition ([`result/scivetti-let-alone-forced-decomposition-v1`](findings/results/scivetti-let-alone-forced-decomposition-v1.md)) returned a **third** outcome the fire/non-fire value model had no slot for — a *directional but underpowered* easing (gpt +0.21, p = 0.090, below baseline; "partially fired / candidate"), neither a clean fire nor a clean miss. The deepening adds the partial-witness slot and a **power-up scope clause**: its correct continuation is a **powered re-run of the same axis** (more items), which the "axis novelty / same axis twice" and parent-essay "more of the same probe cannot" cautions would wrongly forbid — the discriminator being **whether the first run produced a directional effect** (powering a *signal* resolves statistics, not the existence question a clean non-witness already answered); the exemption is narrow and self-extinguishing, and closure ≠ suspension is untouched (a partial witness keeps the search live). **No new empirical claim; no human comparison.** `refines` [`essay/undischargeable-negative`](findings/essays/undischargeable-negative.md); `depends-on` [`essay/capability-split`](findings/essays/capability-split.md) + [`essay/transcript-ceiling`](findings/essays/transcript-ceiling.md) + [`result/relational-order-composition-c-easier-k4`](findings/results/relational-order-composition-c-easier-k4.md) + [`result/relational-order-composition-c-figure-to-figure`](findings/results/relational-order-composition-c-figure-to-figure.md) + [`result/scivetti-let-alone-forced-decomposition-v1`](findings/results/scivetti-let-alone-forced-decomposition-v1.md) + [`essay/output-channel-confound`](findings/essays/output-channel-confound.md) + [`concept/formal-vs-functional-competence`](base/concepts/formal-vs-functional-competence.md); `contingent-on: []`. (**methodological / philosophical track**)
- [`findings/essays/floor-is-not-a-ceiling.md`](findings/essays/floor-is-not-a-ceiling.md) — status: **draft** (2026-06-19); **the project's FOURTEENTH essay** (methodological / philosophical track), the **refinement** of the thirteenth ([`essay/witness-seeking-economics`](findings/essays/witness-seeking-economics.md)). It **answers that essay's revision trigger (b)** — does a **structural bound** (kind-3 reach-closure) exist for *thin-side* two-move composition? — and answers it **in the negative; the negative is the contribution**. The composition witness-search is now suspended across **four** instruments with the structural bound recorded as "**none yet**" ([`result/relational-order-composition-c-worked-example`](findings/results/relational-order-composition-c-worked-example.md) item (iii)); this essay asks whether the **≥2-move floor** (a composition needs ≥2 moves) plus the behavioral localization of the difficulty to "chaining execution" can be turned into a kind-3 bound, and shows it **cannot**, on three grounds: **(A)** the candidate bound's load-bearing premise ("the difficulty *is* the irreducible core") is a **behavioral universal** undischargeable per [`essay/undischargeable-negative`](findings/essays/undischargeable-negative.md) — it is "M cannot chain" disguised as a structural argument (a **kind-4 smuggle**, refused); **(B)** the ≥2-move floor bounds only the *step-count* axis, leaving the elicitation space **open** along un-eased axes (a different/more-familiar non-commuting operation pair, execution-format scaffolding, many-shot); **(C)** — the **original contribution** — a **task-parameter floor** is the wrong *type* of object to be a reach-closure. The criterion: *a kind-3 reach-closure excludes the witness from an entire instrument **class** by a class-level (typically definitional, medium-level) property (the transcript ceiling: the rich-side surplus is constitutively absent from any record); a bound on a **task parameter** caps one knob and leaves the witness-bearing region (≥2 moves, open along other axes) populated — **not every floor is a ceiling.*** Verdict: **no kind-3 bound of the available type exists**, so the composition witness-search can only ever be **suspended on budget, never structurally closed** — upgrading the result's item-(iii) "none yet" from a placeholder to a **reasoned null**. **Sharpens** witness-seeking-economics (adds the gate a candidate bound must pass to count as structural) and **reinforces** the closure ≠ suspension line (guards against a parameter floor masquerading as a reach-closure). Leaves a **non-behavioral** capacity-closure open (undischargeable-negative trigger (a)). **No new empirical claim; no human comparison** (`internal-contrast-only` result read at strength). `refines` [`essay/witness-seeking-economics`](findings/essays/witness-seeking-economics.md); `depends-on` [`essay/undischargeable-negative`](findings/essays/undischargeable-negative.md) + [`essay/transcript-ceiling`](findings/essays/transcript-ceiling.md) + [`essay/capability-split`](findings/essays/capability-split.md) + [`result/relational-order-composition-c-worked-example`](findings/results/relational-order-composition-c-worked-example.md) + [`concept/formal-vs-functional-competence`](base/concepts/formal-vs-functional-competence.md); `contingent-on: []`. (**methodological / philosophical track**)
- [`findings/essays/output-channel-confound.md`](findings/essays/output-channel-confound.md) — status: **draft** (2026-06-19); **the project's FIFTEENTH essay** (methodological / philosophical track), the **refinement** of the twelfth ([`essay/undischargeable-negative`](findings/essays/undischargeable-negative.md)) and thirteenth ([`essay/witness-seeking-economics`](findings/essays/witness-seeking-economics.md)), written off the 38th-session **witness** ([`result/relational-order-composition-c-reasoning-scaffold`](findings/results/relational-order-composition-c-reasoning-scaffold.md)). Names a confound: the **output channel** through which a model must answer — a forced single token vs. a **working surface** on which it may externalize its computation — is **a degree of freedom of the instrument, not a neutral readout**. A channel too narrow to carry a multi-step computation can **mask** a capability the model has (the four-instrument composition split **dissolved** into panel-concordance when the channel alone was widened, reasoning-effort held constant); a wide channel can **scaffold** one. So there is **no neutral channel**, a behavioral capability claim is **indexed to a channel**, and an unindexed one is underspecified. Methodological upshots: a forced-format capability-**negative** is, until the channel is varied, **channel-bounded, never a capacity verdict** (the kind-2 verdict was a true measurement of a *channel-bounded* capability — the error the confound names is **mis-description**, not false measurement — preserving [`essay/undischargeable-negative`](findings/essays/undischargeable-negative.md)); the channel is therefore a **mandatory, high-value control** the [`essay/witness-seeking-economics`](findings/essays/witness-seeking-economics.md) allocation should rank among the **first** easings, not last (cheap; recurs across the instrument library; was the *decisive* axis here). **Scoped**: the confound bites only when the probed capability requires **serial, externalizable** computation **and** the channel forbids externalizing it — so single-token *tasks* (acceptability, single-premise NLI) are untouched. Draws a **machine performance/competence** map (the aperture is a performance constraint masking a competence — a frame, no human claim) and an **aperture-vs-ceiling dual** with [`essay/transcript-ceiling`](findings/essays/transcript-ceiling.md) (input-medium ceiling vs. output-channel aperture; the two errors — ceiling-mistaken-for-aperture vs. aperture-mistaken-for-ceiling — are opposite ends of one instrument). Generalizes the single execution-format axis [`essay/floor-is-not-a-ceiling`](findings/essays/floor-is-not-a-ceiling.md) objection (B) merely named. **No new empirical claim; no human comparison** (`internal-contrast-only` result read at strength). `refines` [`essay/undischargeable-negative`](findings/essays/undischargeable-negative.md) + [`essay/witness-seeking-economics`](findings/essays/witness-seeking-economics.md); `depends-on` [`essay/floor-is-not-a-ceiling`](findings/essays/floor-is-not-a-ceiling.md) + [`essay/capability-split`](findings/essays/capability-split.md) + [`essay/transcript-ceiling`](findings/essays/transcript-ceiling.md) + [`result/relational-order-composition-c-reasoning-scaffold`](findings/results/relational-order-composition-c-reasoning-scaffold.md) + [`concept/formal-vs-functional-competence`](base/concepts/formal-vs-functional-competence.md); `contingent-on: []`. (**methodological / philosophical track**)
- [`findings/essays/concordant-verdict-hides-spread.md`](findings/essays/concordant-verdict-hides-spread.md) — status: **revised** (2026-06-20; revision logged session 53 — the fresh-item replication [`result/dative-information-structure-v2`](findings/results/dative-information-structure-v2.md) fired revision trigger (c) in the **strengthening** direction: the spread did NOT compress (gemini-to-gpt ≈9×→≈27×), gpt's v1 CONFIRM dropped to WEAK, so v1's concordant 3/3 demonstrably hid a fragile member — the essay's empirical spine is firmer, its discipline unchanged, the "wants replication" caveat discharged); **the project's SIXTEENTH essay** (methodological / philosophical track), the **refinement** of the eleventh ([`essay/capability-split`](findings/essays/capability-split.md)) into the **concordant** case that essay left open ("*A concordant verdict may license a cautious panel-scoped sentence*"). Written off the session-51 dative result ([`result/dative-information-structure-v1`](findings/results/dative-information-structure-v1.md)), the project's first human-anchored Tier-2 positive — a **CONCORDANT CONFIRM (3/3)** that nonetheless sits on an **order-of-magnitude effect-size spread** (gemini +0.524 ≫ claude +0.327 ≫ gpt +0.056, all clearing their bootstrap lower bound). Original contribution, a **reading discipline**: a binary panel verdict is a **threshold gate**, blind above the threshold, so the shared label "CONFIRM" can hide a wide magnitude spread; and because the dative conjecture's **prediction 3** (effect size *"decorrelates from surface accuracy"*) **confirmed**, the magnitude carries information the label discards. The fence: **a concordant verdict carries its spread** — report per-model magnitudes, mark them **tight vs decorrelated**, and read a wide-spread concordant CONFIRM as licensing the panel-scoped **direction/existence** sentence (*all three track X in the human direction*) but **not** a panel-scoped **magnitude/uniformity** sentence (*the models track X to a similar degree* / *at a rate of …*). Distinguishes **two textures of hidden heterogeneity** — magnitude decorrelation on one instrument (dative) vs across-instrument **convergence heterogeneity** (the AANN PARTIAL, via [`open-question/instrument-sensitivity-constructional-inference`](findings/open-questions/instrument-sensitivity-constructional-inference.md)) — and locates the bite at the **functional** end of the formal/functional cut ([`claim/formal-competence-aann-ceiling`](findings/claims/formal-competence-aann-ceiling.md) the tight-concord formal contrast). **Not a model ranking** (prediction 3 decorrelates magnitude from competence; no in-repo cross-task tabulation), **no human magnitude comparison** (only the dative *direction* is human-anchored), **"comparable general competence" flagged an unmeasured background premise**. `refines` [`essay/capability-split`](findings/essays/capability-split.md); `depends-on` [`result/dative-information-structure-v1`](findings/results/dative-information-structure-v1.md) + [`conjecture/dative-alternation-information-structure`](findings/conjectures/dative-alternation-information-structure.md) + [`open-question/instrument-sensitivity-constructional-inference`](findings/open-questions/instrument-sensitivity-constructional-inference.md) + [`concept/formal-vs-functional-competence`](base/concepts/formal-vs-functional-competence.md); `contingent-on: []`. **2026-06-21 (session 63):** a measurement-level sibling was named — [`essay/point-estimate-is-a-draw`](findings/essays/point-estimate-is-a-draw.md) adds the prior question this essay's per-model-magnitude comparison presupposes (*is the smaller magnitude bigger than its own run-to-run jitter?*); **no clause changed**, the "single run" honesty-box caveat given a named mechanism. (**methodological / philosophical track**)
- [`findings/essays/point-estimate-is-a-draw.md`](findings/essays/point-estimate-is-a-draw.md) — status: **revised** (2026-06-21, session 64 — **trigger (a) FIRED**; originally draft session 63); **the project's SEVENTEENTH essay** (methodological / philosophical track), the **measurement-level** sibling of the sixteenth ([`essay/concordant-verdict-hides-spread`](findings/essays/concordant-verdict-hides-spread.md)) and eleventh ([`essay/capability-split`](findings/essays/capability-split.md)) — those two are about variation in the **phenomenon** (between-model split; between-model magnitude decorrelation); this one is one level down, about variation in the **measurement**. Written off the session-62 powered let-alone re-run ([`result/scivetti-let-alone-powered-rerun-v1`](findings/results/scivetti-let-alone-powered-rerun-v1.md)), which ran a **byte-identical** instrument twice and found temperature-0 labels are **not** reproducible (claude 0.833→0.708 on the *identical* 24 items via 3 adverse flips; gpt 3/24 flips netting 0; **gemini deterministic**). Original contribution, a **reading discipline**: a single-run accuracy at temp 0 is a **draw**, not a fixed quantity, so it carries a **run-to-run jitter** that single-run Wilson/bootstrap CIs (which assume a fixed per-item Bernoulli rate) **structurally understate**; therefore **a between-X gap no larger than the jitter floor is not yet a finding** — rest weight on a small effect only if it clears the plausible jitter or the jitter is measured by repeated runs. Threads the needle with [`essay/undischargeable-negative`](findings/essays/undischargeable-negative.md): re-running the same hard instrument to "firm up" a null buys nothing, but re-running to **measure the noise floor** is licit (the trigger-(g) redirect). Bite is **uneven by design** — hardest at **small functional effects** ([`concept/formal-vs-functional-competence`](base/concepts/formal-vs-functional-competence.md) end, where the ~±0.12 rivalled the effect), barely at all at **ceilings / clean separations** (the comp-correlative control PRESERVED 1.000; gemini deterministic), and **model-/instrument-specific** (not a transferable constant). **No new empirical claim, no human comparison.** Revision triggers: a repeated-run measurement on a non-near-chance instrument (would narrow the bite to hard/near-chance constructions); jitter shown to be a transferable constant (would harden into a numeric correction); an open-access source on temp-0 nondeterminism entering the repo (would ground the mechanism — queued in `wanted.md`, **not** in-repo, **not** fabricated); a small-but-real effect re-run and found stable (graduates it past this read). **Revision (session 64): trigger (a) FIRED** — [`result/scivetti-let-alone-repeated-runs-v1`](findings/results/scivetti-let-alone-repeated-runs-v1.md) ran the byte-identical instrument **K=5** and **narrowed** the essay: jitter is **ceiling-protected** (comp-corr range 0.000 vs let-alone up to 0.121) → "draws **on hard near-chance functional instruments**"; **model-specific** (gpt ~±0.12 / claude ~0.06 / gemini ~0.03; trigger (b) un-fired); "gemini deterministic" → "**most stable**" (2/33 churn); and gpt's residual **survives** the jitter (trigger (d) case: de-noised majority-vote 0.606, every one of 5 runs < 0.90). `refines` [`essay/concordant-verdict-hides-spread`](findings/essays/concordant-verdict-hides-spread.md); `depends-on` [`result/scivetti-let-alone-powered-rerun-v1`](findings/results/scivetti-let-alone-powered-rerun-v1.md) + [`result/scivetti-let-alone-repeated-runs-v1`](findings/results/scivetti-let-alone-repeated-runs-v1.md) + [`essay/capability-split`](findings/essays/capability-split.md) + [`essay/witness-seeking-economics`](findings/essays/witness-seeking-economics.md) + [`essay/undischargeable-negative`](findings/essays/undischargeable-negative.md) + [`concept/formal-vs-functional-competence`](base/concepts/formal-vs-functional-competence.md); `contingent-on: []`. (**methodological / philosophical track**)
- [`findings/essays/design-out-not-model-out.md`](findings/essays/design-out-not-model-out.md) — status: **draft** (2026-06-21, session 69); **the project's EIGHTEENTH essay** (methodological / philosophical track). Original contribution, a **design-epistemics rule** drawn from the function-word probe's session-68 overturn: **a control covariate that is *degenerate* — zero (or near-zero) within-condition variance, hence perfectly collinear with the manipulation — cannot be "controlled for" by regression or stratification; it must be designed out at construction time, not modelled out at analysis time.** Worked case: the function-word swap's orthographic length-delta is constant (+1) in the function arm, so stratifying collapses to the hard-matched set and regression identifies the contrast only off the +1 stratum — the length-neutral items a relaxation would add **never enter the bearing contrast** (the reason [`decisions/resolved/function-word-count-vs-matching`](decisions/resolved/function-word-count-vs-matching.md) overturned the relax-length default). Draws the **line** at within-condition variance (comfortable case: variance present → statistical control fine; **genuinely hard middle**: tiny-but-nonzero variance → burden shifts to construction; degenerate: design-out is the only valid control) and prices the **cost** (design-out constrains stimulus supply — the operationalization-vs-power tension, in the probe's own collapse numbers). `refines` [`essay/point-estimate-is-a-draw`](findings/essays/point-estimate-is-a-draw.md) ("analysis cannot manufacture information the design did not put there") + [`essay/output-channel-confound`](findings/essays/output-channel-confound.md) (a parameter that must be *fixed* vs one that must be *varied* to be read); `depends-on` [`resource/subtlex-us-frequency`](base/resources/subtlex-us-frequency.md) + [`conjecture/function-word-substitutability`](findings/conjectures/function-word-substitutability.md). **No new empirical claim, no human comparison** (`internal-contrast-only` probe). (**methodological / philosophical track**)
- [`findings/essays/graded-scale-ungraded-commitment.md`](findings/essays/graded-scale-ungraded-commitment.md) — status: **draft** (2026-06-21, session 75); **the project's NINETEENTH essay** (lexical / philosophical track), written in the interval between the now-ratified lexical bridging-context design and its (unrun) probe. Original contribution, a conceptual distinction: a **graded sense scale** (cross-item: the model rank-orders usage pairs the way humans do — what [`result/lexical-sense-gradience-v1`](findings/results/lexical-sense-gradience-v1.md) established) and **graded sense commitment** (within-item: lower confidence / declined binary on the single genuinely-ambiguous use — the unrun Prediction 4) are **logically independent**; v1 established only the former. Argues the first-class **null** — "graded scale, **ungraded** commitment," a smooth relatedness ordering with a confident discrete pick on every individual bridging use — is a **substantive behavioral finding** about machine sense (gradience in the aggregate ledger, none in the moment), contrasted against the lexicographer's *individual* indeterminacy on bridging uses. Frames the within-item distributional shadow as **three** live outcomes (commitment that survives the context control / ungraded commitment / commitment that evaporates under the control), and ties the fork to what distributional competence recovers ([`concept/distributional-meaning`](base/concepts/distributional-meaning.md), [`concept/referential-meaning`](base/concepts/referential-meaning.md)). Three load-bearing disciplines: **behavior, not representation**; **usage-similarity, not certified sense co-presence** (the ratified anchor cap); the **contrast must clear** or there is nothing to read. Four revision triggers (positive-survives-control / the null / B–C disagreement-or-Route-3-collapse / a representational instrument); honesty box. **No new empirical claim, no human comparison beyond v1's usage-similarity-capped cross-item monotonicity.** `refines` + `depends-on` [`conjecture/lexical-sense-gradience`](findings/conjectures/lexical-sense-gradience.md); `depends-on` [`result/lexical-sense-gradience-v1`](findings/results/lexical-sense-gradience-v1.md) + [`open-question/lexical-bridging-context-gradience`](findings/open-questions/lexical-bridging-context-gradience.md) + [`concept/polysemy`](base/concepts/polysemy.md) + [`concept/referential-meaning`](base/concepts/referential-meaning.md) + [`concept/distributional-meaning`](base/concepts/distributional-meaning.md); `contingent-on: []`. (**lexical / philosophical track**)
- [`findings/essays/no-admissible-certifier.md`](findings/essays/no-admissible-certifier.md) — status: **draft** (2026-06-23, session 92); **the project's TWENTIETH essay** (methodological / philosophical track), the generalization of the session-91 forced-both NULL. Original contribution: a behavioral probe's stimulus **premises** must be certified by a **certifier tripod** — independent of the model under test (anti-circularity), human bearing only via an *existing* resource (no human subjects), in place before the run — and when a *required* premise is readable **only** by a fresh human subject or the model-under-test, with no pre-encoding resource, it has **no admissible certifier** and the item is **uncertifiable from in-repo means**. Worked case: the forced-both in-item balance check ([`result/forced-both-lexical-build-attempt-v1`](findings/results/forced-both-lexical-build-attempt-v1.md)). Placed as a **third** thing, distinct from [`essay/undischargeable-negative`](findings/essays/undischargeable-negative.md) (conclusion-side) and [`essay/design-out-not-model-out`](findings/essays/design-out-not-model-out.md) (which assumes a construction-time fix); the **escape is the anchor discipline** (an existing human-labeled resource), the **honest price** of two good rules (no-human-subjects + anti-circularity). **Trigger (a) partially exercised the same session** by the SemEval co-activation scout ([`resource/semeval2017-pun-corpus`](base/resources/semeval2017-pun-corpus.md)): the escape lifts *co-activation* (via stimulus redesign), but the *in-item balance* premise still has no admissible certifier — confirmation, not refutation. `refines` [`essay/design-out-not-model-out`](findings/essays/design-out-not-model-out.md); `depends-on` [`essay/undischargeable-negative`](findings/essays/undischargeable-negative.md) + [`result/forced-both-lexical-build-attempt-v1`](findings/results/forced-both-lexical-build-attempt-v1.md) + [`essay/layer-specialness-vs-always-resolvability`](findings/essays/layer-specialness-vs-always-resolvability.md). **No new empirical claim; no human comparison.** (created 2026-06-23; **methodological / philosophical track**)
- [`findings/essays/presence-is-not-balance.md`](findings/essays/presence-is-not-balance.md) — status: **revised** (2026-06-23, session 93; trigger (b) attempted-and-not-met logged session 94 — the forced-both v2 build tried the argued transfer-to-item and a fresh critic ruled it not arguable, fresh corroboration of the essay's core); **the project's TWENTY-FIRST essay** (lexical / methodological track), generalizing the session-93 ratification of [`decisions/resolved/sense-coactivation-anchor-semeval-puns`](decisions/resolved/sense-coactivation-anchor-semeval-puns.md). Original contribution: a distinction between a **co-presence premise** (two senses are both in play in an item — existential, on/off) and a **balance premise** (neither of the two dominates — relative, graded), and the **asymmetry** that an *attested* ambiguity discharges the first and is **silent by type** on the second (a presence record is the wrong object to measure a salience weighting). Vivid case: a homographic pun *guarantees* co-presence (the joint requirement makes the joke) yet the genre's setup/punchline mechanics *bias against* balance, so the resource that best certifies co-presence is among the worst-placed to certify no-dominance. **Anchor rule** that follows: a resource may soundly anchor co-presence while *inventing* an anchor for balance, so the two must be sourced separately and the balance source must be graded and item-transferable (the word-grain [`resource/homonym-meaning-dominance-norms`](base/resources/homonym-meaning-dominance-norms.md) is the right *type* but still owes an argued transfer-to-item step). `refines` [`essay/no-admissible-certifier`](findings/essays/no-admissible-certifier.md) (sharpens its escape: arriving-certified is **premise-relative**); serves [`essay/layer-specialness-vs-always-resolvability`](findings/essays/layer-specialness-vs-always-resolvability.md) (why Q1-ii's separate dominance step is type-correctness, not caution). `depends-on` the two resolved decisions + [`result/forced-both-lexical-build-attempt-v1`](findings/results/forced-both-lexical-build-attempt-v1.md) + [`resource/semeval2017-pun-corpus`](base/resources/semeval2017-pun-corpus.md) + [`resource/homonym-meaning-dominance-norms`](base/resources/homonym-meaning-dominance-norms.md) + [`concept/polysemy`](base/concepts/polysemy.md). Four revision triggers; honesty box. **No new empirical claim; no human comparison.** (created 2026-06-23; **lexical / methodological track**)
- [`findings/essays/construct-validity-without-a-criterion.md`](findings/essays/construct-validity-without-a-criterion.md) — status: **revised** (2026-06-23 created session 95; revised through 2026-06-24 session 98 — trigger (d) fired s96, trigger (e) FULLY DISCHARGED s97 Borsboom + s98 Campbell & Fiske); **the project's TWENTY-SECOND essay** (methodological / philosophical track). Original contribution, a **reframing-plus-diagnosis**: the project's accumulated operationalization-gate discipline (freeze-before-run, `internal-contrast-only`, "no admissible certifier," "design-out-not-model-out," "presence-is-not-balance") **is** construct validation in [`source/cronbach-meehl-1955-construct-validity`](base/sources/cronbach-meehl-1955-construct-validity.md)'s sense, and the **no-human-subjects rule removes the criterion-oriented leg by rule** (predictive/concurrent validation needs "an independent criterion measure on the same subjects"; the project's subjects are models and fresh human subjects are barred), leaving **nomological-net construct validity as the only available form**. That single fact **predicts** the project's four recurring terminal states: `internal-contrast-only` = construct validity with the criterion leg amputated; "no admissible certifier" = a missing **observable node** in the net (Cronbach & Meehl's admissibility principle 3); the **two-edged negative** = disconfirmation falling on the whole net (their three-way charge — test / theory / design, "any link in the chain may be wrong" — the classical form of [`essay/undischargeable-negative`](findings/essays/undischargeable-negative.md)'s typology); design-out / presence-is-not-balance = construct-instrument correspondence hygiene. Identifies [`essay/cross-level-convergence-ladder`](findings/essays/cross-level-convergence-ladder.md) as the project's **nomological-net-elaboration engine** (principle 4: "'Learning more about' a … construct is … elaborating the nomological network"). The honest price: without a criterion nothing outside the net pins the construct, so the freeze-and-rung discipline is load-bearing, and the criterion leg was **surrendered on purpose** for auditable anchoring. `refines` [`essay/no-admissible-certifier`](findings/essays/no-admissible-certifier.md) + [`essay/design-out-not-model-out`](findings/essays/design-out-not-model-out.md); `depends-on` [`source/cronbach-meehl-1955-construct-validity`](base/sources/cronbach-meehl-1955-construct-validity.md) + [`essay/undischargeable-negative`](findings/essays/undischargeable-negative.md) + [`essay/presence-is-not-balance`](findings/essays/presence-is-not-balance.md) + [`essay/cross-level-convergence-ladder`](findings/essays/cross-level-convergence-ladder.md). **Revised 2026-06-24 (session 96 — trigger (d) FIRED):** two post-1955 validity sources ingested — [`source/messick-1995-validity-of-psychological-assessment`](base/sources/messick-1995-validity-of-psychological-assessment.md) (now the essay states its *design-out → construct-irrelevant-variance* and *presence-is-not-balance → construct-underrepresentation* mappings in Messick's **verbatim, sourced** vocabulary) and [`source/freiesleben-2026-construct-validity-llm-benchmarks`](base/sources/freiesleben-2026-construct-validity-llm-benchmarks.md) (an independent measurement-philosophy preprint making the project's own framing choice — nomological net over causal/inferential — for LLM capability benchmarks). New section "Does the reconstruction match the post-1955 consensus?" answers: **largely yes** (Messick's unification, with the project as a limiting case; Freiesleben's LLM-domain corroboration), with one honest **gap** (the consequential/value aspect Messick adds, untheorized here) and one new **sharpening** — a *second amputation*: the project is barred from Borsboom's **causal/realist** validation leg too (it declines to assert the construct lives in the model), so the nomological net is the only one of the three classical routes its constraints leave available. **Revised 2026-06-24 (session 97 — trigger (e) Borsboom leg) + (session 98 — trigger (e) Campbell & Fiske leg):** both validity primaries are now in-repo, so trigger (e) is **fully discharged** — the causal/realist "second amputation" leg cites [`source/borsboom-2004-concept-of-validity`](base/sources/borsboom-2004-concept-of-validity.md) directly (s97), and the convergent/discriminant + multitrait–multimethod vocabulary cites [`source/campbell-fiske-1959-mtmm`](base/sources/campbell-fiske-1959-mtmm.md) directly (s98), each a secondary→primary upgrade with the secondary characterizations confirmed consistent (no correction). The essay now rests on five methodology primaries; **only trigger (f)** (the consequential/value aspect) stays dormant. `depends-on` the validity primaries added. **No new empirical claim; no human comparison** (methodology sources, not human-comparison anchors). (created 2026-06-23; revised through 2026-06-24; **methodological / philosophical track**)

### Findings — claims / results / theory / open-questions

- [`findings/claims/formal-competence-aann-ceiling.md`](findings/claims/formal-competence-aann-ceiling.md) — status: proposed (2026-05-28); AANN acceptability ceiling is evidence of formal, not functional, linguistic competence. Grounded by Mahowald 2024 formal/functional distinction; anchored to [`resource/mahowald-2023-aann-stimuli`](base/resources/mahowald-2023-aann-stimuli.md).
- [`findings/claims/constructional-divergent-form-generalization-gap.md`](findings/claims/constructional-divergent-form-generalization-gap.md) — status: proposed (2026-05-29); LLMs track constructional form–meaning pairings "up to a point" but show a >40% generalization gap (GPT-o1) on syntactically-identical / semantically-divergent forms vs. a native-speaker baseline (≈0.90/≈0.83). The project's first claim with in-repo human-comparison empirical bearing. Anchored to [`resource/scivetti-2025-cxnli-dataset`](base/resources/scivetti-2025-cxnli-dataset.md); sits at the theory ladder's Tier 3→4 boundary. `contingent-on: []`.
- [`findings/claims/cxg-probing-surprisal-validity.md`](findings/claims/cxg-probing-surprisal-validity.md) — status: proposed (2026-05-29); surprisal contrast on form–meaning minimal pairs is a valid (but bounded) operationalization of constructional-meaning *sensitivity*. Methodological counterpart to the AANN-ceiling claim. Anchored to `resource/mahowald-2023-aann-stimuli` (AANN-scoped); cross-construction generality stays provisional (`cxg-probing-anchor` resolved 2026-05-29, Option A).
- [`findings/claims/preference-commitment-dissociation-aann-specific.md`](findings/claims/preference-commitment-dissociation-aann-specific.md) — status: **supported** (2026-06-15); **the honest close of the generality question** — on the evidence so far, the forced-choice-paraphrase-vs-entailment ("preference without commitment") dissociation is **AANN-specific**. It replicates across two disjoint AANN item sets ([`result/aann-inferential-v4`](findings/results/aann-inferential-v4.md) paraphrase Δ² +0.78/+0.70/+0.96; [`result/aann-inferential-v6`](findings/results/aann-inferential-v6.md) +0.875/+0.575/+0.90) but **does not reproduce on the conative** across two independent verb samples ([`result/conative-preference-commitment-v1`](findings/results/conative-preference-commitment-v1.md) INCONCLUSIVE, Δ²_pref non-positive in all three; [`result/conative-commitment-replication-v2`](findings/results/conative-commitment-replication-v2.md) the lone counter-signal collapsing +0.46→+0.04), **in either direction** — the apparent conative exception was verb-set-specific noise. Draws three calibrated consequences: the dissociation does not generalize beyond AANN on current evidence; a forced-choice "preference" can be driven by a bare lexical cue (so a preference shift is not by itself evidence of constructional inference); the result is construction-particular. Calibrated hard to "AANN-specific *so far*" (only **one** alternative construction tested; a third needs engineered headroom). `anchor: internal-contrast-only` (a within-model cross-construction contrast, inherited from its constituent results; no new human-comparison claim); `contingent-on: []`. Refines [`conjecture/preference-commitment-generality`](findings/conjectures/preference-commitment-generality.md) (tested → not confirmed), [`essay/preference-without-commitment`](findings/essays/preference-without-commitment.md), and the theory ladder. (**grammatical track**)
- [`findings/claims/relational-order-sensitive-reassignment.md`](findings/claims/relational-order-sensitive-reassignment.md) — status: **supported** (2026-06-16, twentieth session); **LLM referential conventions are order-sensitive (non-commutative) when the history carries disambiguating recency information.** Promoted from the clean ceiling positive in [`result/relational-spontaneous-recency-a`](findings/results/relational-spontaneous-recency-a.md): when a coined term is reassigned across stamped rounds so the content-set is symmetric and only recency disambiguates, both models (claude, gemini) recover it by its **most-recent binding** spontaneously (latest-binding 1.000, position at chance, DIRECT on-demand 1.000). **Contradicts** [`conjecture/commutative-convention`](findings/conjectures/commutative-convention.md) (retired); **refines** [`concept/relational-meaning`](base/concepts/relational-meaning.md) (places the models on the order-sensitive side, but at its *bottom rung* — a thin latest-binding-wins rule, not constitution). Scope: internal-contrast-only (no human comparison); one operationalization; thin≠rich; "spontaneous" = query-not-directed, not cue-free. **Strengthened 2026-06-17** by the implicit-reassignment control ([`result/relational-implicit-reassignment-control`](findings/results/relational-implicit-reassignment-control.md)): with the explicit "was reassigned" flag removed, the behaviour persists at ceiling — not a wording artifact (revision trigger 2 bounded, scope limit 4 tightened to *flag-not-directed*). `anchor: internal-contrast-only`; `contingent-on: []`. (**relational axis**)
- [`findings/claims/dative-pronominality-partial-reach.md`](findings/claims/dative-pronominality-partial-reach.md) — status: **supported** (2026-06-20, session 56); **recipient pronominality — the LARGEST information-structure factor in the human dative (−1.48) — is a documented partial-reach (Option C), not a behavioral finding.** Realizes Option C of [`decisions/resolved/dative-pronominality-operationalization`](decisions/resolved/dative-pronominality-operationalization.md): under pure autonomy (no prompt logprobs) **no controlled forced-choice minimal pair isolates pronominality from length and givenness by construction** — a pronoun is a property of the scored sentence (so the within-item length-immunity collapses to a between-item contrast), is intrinsically the shorter constituent (so it reintroduces the short-before-long confound and cannot fill the given-but-longer dissociation cell), and is near-collinear with givenness. The provisional Option-A default (length-matched pronoun-vs-name) was *rejected* — its repeated-name-penalty confound runs in the *predicted* direction and prosodic weight is not dissociable by construction. So pronominality is reported **only on the human side** (where the corpus fit weights it most heavily of the information-structure factors) and left as the documented edge of the instrument's reach — a "text alone cannot reach this" closure analogous to the relational transcript-ceiling and third-construction headroom closures. **No probe, $0; makes no "model can/can't" claim.** Human-anchored to [`resource/languageR-dative-corpus`](base/resources/languageR-dative-corpus.md); bounds [`result/dative-information-structure-v1`](findings/results/dative-information-structure-v1.md)/[`v2`](findings/results/dative-information-structure-v2.md) (the *reached* givenness result, untouched). `anchor: human-anchored`; `contingent-on: []`. (**grammatical track**)
- [`findings/claims/lexical-graded-scale-ungraded-commitment.md`](findings/claims/lexical-graded-scale-ungraded-commitment.md) — status: **supported** (2026-06-22, session 77); **on human-rated usage-similarity-midpoint (bridging) pairs, all three panel models place the pair at an intermediate relatedness position but meet it with clear-item confidence and almost never decline — a graded SCALE with ungraded COMMITMENT** (behavioral; usage-similarity-capped). The empirical statement [`essay/graded-scale-ungraded-commitment`](findings/essays/graded-scale-ungraded-commitment.md) anticipated, now carried by [`result/lexical-bridging-context-v1`](findings/results/lexical-bridging-context-v1.md) (3/3 models; clear-class precondition met; commitment null corroborated across confidence (B), decline (C), and dispersion (A)). Scope/caps: usage-similarity not sense co-presence; behavioral not representational; small lemma-clustered N (24 bridging/17 lemmas); the commitment null is the shadow-robust part, the position/scale reading partly tracks topic (Q3 r 0.32–0.53). Anchored to [`resource/dwug-usage-graphs`](base/resources/dwug-usage-graphs.md) (clear poles supplemented by [`resource/wic-word-in-context`](base/resources/wic-word-in-context.md)); `contingent-on: []`. (**lexical track**)
- [`findings/theory/constructional-meaning-in-llms.md`](findings/theory/constructional-meaning-in-llms.md) — status: draft (updated 2026-05-31); the project's first theory page. A five-tier evidence ladder (form-acceptability < surprisal-contrast < gradient semantic tracking < generalization < inference-licensing) placing each claim/conjecture/result; brackets the grounding axis; flags the relational axis as future work. Holds the eleven own-design constructional results; the 2026-05-31 consolidation discharged the "first lexical probe" revision trigger and brought its lexical/grounding cross-references current (pointing to the continuum page for depth).
- [`findings/theory/lexicon-grammar-continuum.md`](findings/theory/lexicon-grammar-continuum.md) — status: draft (updated 2026-05-31); the project's **second theory page — the lexical↔grammatical connection** (Tom's steer). Argues the lexical and grammatical wedges are the two ends of one CxG form–meaning cline (a word = a maximally specific construction) probed by **one test**: does a meaning gradient beat the distributional shadow (context similarity for words; n-gram/form for constructions)? The project now has a positive that beats the shadow on **both** ends ([`result/lexical-sense-gradience-v1`](findings/results/lexical-sense-gradience-v1.md) + the CC results). The 2026-05-31 consolidation absorbed the full lexical/bridge/grounding state: clause (b) discreteness is a **powered null** (v3), the coercion bridge **partially de-confounds** (v1→v2, fragile fine-scale residual), and the grounding axis stands at **two bounded negatives** (perceptual-moderation + image redundancy). Governs the bridge probe [`design/coercion-as-sense-modulation-v1`](../experiments/designs/coercion-as-sense-modulation-v1.md) (coercion = grammar-induced lexical sense shift).
- [`findings/theory/situating-llm-meaning.md`](findings/theory/situating-llm-meaning.md) — status: draft (created 2026-05-31; **relational cell synced 2026-06-16; enriched 2026-06-19** with the order-sensitive composition rung); the project's **third theory page — the philosophical-map synthesis**. Positions the four axes' findings (constructional ladder, lexical gradience positive, grounding nulls, relational result, cross-axis dissociation) against the classical positions now in the concept layer, stating for each which the evidence **supports / strains / is silent on**. Verdict (a calibrated sketch, not a settled location): LLM meaning, where the project can see it, lives **model-internal** as a graded, compositional, *thin*-inferential **use**-structure that **beats but does not escape** the distributional shadow — while the three between/beyond loci (referential/world, perceptual grounding, between-agents) are each **silent or bounded-negative**; a deflation-leaning but **not** eliminativist picture (the descriptivist middle the charter chose). **2026-06-16:** the relational cell is updated for the Option-A falsification — still **negative on constitution** (the order-sensitivity is thin), but the clean commutative-aggregation reading is now falsified where order disambiguates ([`claim/relational-order-sensitive-reassignment`](findings/claims/relational-order-sensitive-reassignment.md)); the "commutativity stays under perturbation" prediction **resolved against**. `contingent-on: []`.

### Findings — results

- [`findings/results/dative-information-structure-v1.md`](findings/results/dative-information-structure-v1.md) — status: proposed (2026-06-20, session 51); **the dative alternation tracks information structure — a human-anchored Tier-2 panel CONFIRM (3/3).** Runs the frozen+certified instrument ([`stimuli.json` sha `0ffe3700…ababf`]) under the ratified operationalization [`decisions/resolved/dative-anchor-and-indicator`](decisions/resolved/dative-anchor-and-indicator.md). All three panel models shift double-object-vs-prepositional-dative preference in the **human direction** (given recipient → DOC, given theme → PD) across a manipulation that holds length+animacy **identical by construction** (within-item shift provably immune to every length/position/order shortcut — build-certified, all 8 shortcut readers → shift 0), and the effect **survives the end-weight dissociation control** (given = the *longer* constituent) for all three. **Effect size sharply decorrelated** (gemini +0.524 ≫ claude +0.327 ≫ gpt +0.056, all bootstrap-LB > 0 → prediction 3 confirmed; gpt a weak-but-clearing CONFIRM). Secondary corpus-gradient Spearman ρ 0.48–0.83 (non-decisive, strengthens). 0 NA/retry/trunc; independent post-run verifier REPRODUCED from raw. Human-anchored to [`resource/languageR-dative-corpus`](base/resources/languageR-dative-corpus.md) (Bresnan et al. 2007 production surface). $1.578 billed (a disclosed $1.50 hard-stop-and-resume on gpt — budget gate, blind to analysis; total under the $5/day cap). The project's **first human-anchored Tier-2 positive of its own design**; the grammatical core returns. (created 2026-06-20)

So the panel verdict is **CONFIRM 2/3, not v1's 3/3**, the gemini-to-gpt magnitude ratio **widens ≈9×→≈27×** (spread did not compress), and **v1's concordant 3/3 hid the one fragile member** whose CONFIRM did not survive replication — exactly the case [`essay/concordant-verdict-hides-spread`](findings/essays/concordant-verdict-hides-spread.md) is built to catch (its revision trigger (c) fired in the strengthening direction; logged revision, `draft`→`revised`). - [`findings/results/function-word-swap-build-v1.md`](findings/results/function-word-swap-build-v1.md) — status: proposed (2026-06-21, session 67; **corrected session 68**); **a BUILD / feasibility result (no model run, $0): the function-word swap probe is a certified NO-GO because faithful frequency+length matching starves the matched set.** The frozen set passes minimal-pair integrity, the **length-only-reader** check (asymmetry **0.0** — content swaps must match the function swaps' signed **+1** length) and no-leak, but `certification.json` is `"ok": false` on **three** checks: **count** (66 < 200), **≥4-class span** (3 viable classes — adjective dead), **and the freq-only reader** (0.1212 > 0.12 — the `because`-arm content gap 1.335 < function gap 1.406). *(The session-67 wording "sound on every shortcut check / fails only the count" overstated it; corrected session 68.)* Three structural facts: the **person-noun route dies**; **`the`→`a` admits NO frequency-matched content control** (no content word reaches Lg10WF ≈ 6.0); `some`/`will` each yield a single matched out-word. An **independent reviewer confirmed the NO-GO**. The matching-vs-power tension is **resolved** [`decisions/resolved/function-word-count-vs-matching`](decisions/resolved/function-word-count-vs-matching.md) (session 68 — overturned relax-length; widen the inventory + fix the freq residual); the conjecture stays `designed`, untested. Makes **no claim about LLM behavior**. `refines` [`conjecture/function-word-substitutability`](findings/conjectures/function-word-substitutability.md); `depends-on` [`resource/subtlex-us-frequency`](base/resources/subtlex-us-frequency.md); `anchor: internal-contrast-only`; `contingent-on: []`. - [`findings/results/function-word-swap-run-v2.md`](findings/results/function-word-swap-run-v2.md) — status: supported (2026-06-21, session 69); **the first MODEL result for the function-word conjecture: CONFIRM 3/3, non-uniformly.** Build-v2's frozen 206-item set (4 content classes; arms because/some/will/few; file sha `4763740e…`, certified max-positive shortcut asymmetry 0.0; two fresh pre-run critics NO-GO→GO; $0.502 billed; post-run verifier reproduced every number to the digit). **All three panel models CONFIRM** (claude contrast +0.340 [0.277,0.408]; gpt +0.825 [0.767,0.879]; gemini +0.859 [0.811,0.903]): function-word swaps flip 3-way NLI far more than frequency+length-matched content-word swaps, with the matched-content control near-floor (content flip 1.0/4.4/3.4%; **falsify arm did not fire**). **Non-uniform across function-word types:** `because`→`although` (+1.0/+0.875/+1.0) and `some`→`every` (+0.929/+0.75/+0.75) strong & panel-consistent; **`will`→`would` near-null in all three** (modal future→conditional doesn't shift the inference); **`few`→`many` splits the panel** — claude +0.095 vs gpt/gemini +0.96. Because `few` is 126/206 (61%), the pooled magnitude is dominated by it (claude's low pooled +0.34 is its near-null few arm dragging down a ceiling because/some signal). Prediction 3 holds at the content-CLASS level (all 4 classes fn>ct/model) but **not** the function-TYPE level. `supports` [`conjecture/function-word-substitutability`](findings/conjectures/function-word-substitutability.md); `refines` [`result/function-word-swap-build-v1`](findings/results/function-word-swap-build-v1.md); `depends-on` [`resource/subtlex-us-frequency`](base/resources/subtlex-us-frequency.md); `anchor: internal-contrast-only`; `contingent-on: []`. - [`findings/results/function-word-few-many-split.md`](findings/results/function-word-few-many-split.md) — status: supported (2026-06-21, session 70); **a within-model re-analysis (no spend) localizing run-v2's `few`→`many` panel split to ONE quantifier reading.** Re-reads the in-repo raw NLI from [`result/function-word-swap-run-v2`](findings/results/function-word-swap-run-v2.md) (script `few-arm-split.py`): on the 126 `few`-arm items, **all three models unanimously read "Few X → All X" as a contradiction** (claude 126/126, gpt 125/126, gemini 126/126) — the split is **not** there. The **entire** divergence is on **"Many X → All X"**: claude keeps it a **contradiction** (114/126 ≈ 90%; con→con), gpt (122/126) and gemini (121/126) relax it to **neutral** (con→neu). Reading: claude's labels are consistent with a **scalar-bounded** *many* ("many **but not all**" → contradicts *all*); gpt/gemini with a **lower-bounded-only** *many* ("many, possibly all" → neutral). A concentrated, near-deterministic interpretive divergence (vastly exceeding temp-0 jitter), not noise — which is why the 61% `few` arm drags claude's pooled magnitude down. **Asserts nothing about which reading is correct; no human comparison.** `refines` [`result/function-word-swap-run-v2`](findings/results/function-word-swap-run-v2.md); `supports` [`essay/function-words-not-one-category`](findings/essays/function-words-not-one-category.md); `depends-on` [`conjecture/function-word-substitutability`](findings/conjectures/function-word-substitutability.md) + [`resource/subtlex-us-frequency`](base/resources/subtlex-us-frequency.md) + [`concept/constructional-meaning`](base/concepts/constructional-meaning.md); `anchor: internal-contrast-only`; `contingent-on: []`. (**grammatical/lexical track**)
- [`findings/results/function-word-modal-widening.md`](findings/results/function-word-modal-widening.md) — status: supported (2026-06-21, session 71); **the `will`→`would` modal NLI null does NOT generalize — it is a future→conditional fact, not a modal fact.** Widens the modal arm of [`result/function-word-swap-run-v2`](findings/results/function-word-swap-run-v2.md) to fire essay revision trigger (a). Frozen+certified 118-item / 5-arm set (file sha `cccac581…`, max-positive shortcut asymmetry 0.0; independent pre-run critic GO with its own 9001-pt sweep; $0.2792 billed, 0 unparsed; independent post-run verifier reproduced). Per-arm flip_fn: **`will`→`would` replicates the null** (claude 0/20, gpt 0/20, gemini 3/20); **`must`→`might` (necessity→possibility) flips at CEILING in all three** (20/20 each); **`shall`→`should` (deontic obligation→advisory) SPLITS the panel** (gemini 0.778 reads *should* ≠ *required*; claude/gpt 0.056 collapse *should* ≈ *required*) — base-label agreement HIGH for every modal arm (1.0/1.0/0.89 for shall), so the nulls and split are interpretable, not measurement failures; controls because/some flip ~0.93–1.0, content control near-floor. The instrument registers a modal swap in proportion to how truth-conditionally "loud" it is: loud category-mismatch (must→might, all) > within-deontic-strength (shall→should, one model) > subtle future→conditional irrealis (will→would, none). **Caveat:** must→might crosses deontic→epistemic flavor (a category mismatch, the easy non-entailment) so it does NOT isolate a pure necessity-vs-possibility reading; shall→should is the clean within-scale test. Narrows the essay's blanket "modals are NLI-invisible" reading; vindicates its deeper "the instrument's calibration co-determines the result." Coherence echo: claude (and here gemini) read *some*→all as contradiction (scalar upper-bounding, cf. [`result/function-word-few-many-split`](findings/results/function-word-few-many-split.md)). `refines` [`essay/function-words-not-one-category`](findings/essays/function-words-not-one-category.md) + [`result/function-word-swap-run-v2`](findings/results/function-word-swap-run-v2.md); `depends-on` [`resource/subtlex-us-frequency`](base/resources/subtlex-us-frequency.md); `anchor: internal-contrast-only`; `contingent-on: []`. (**grammatical/lexical track**)

A **fresh independent reviewer** returned **VERDICT-SOUND** (the wall is real, pre-registered, not result-motivated). - [`findings/results/instrument-disagreement-reanalysis-v1.md`](findings/results/instrument-disagreement-reanalysis-v1.md) — status: proposed (2026-05-30); **read-only re-analysis** (no new data, no API spend, $0.00) of the two existing both-instrument runs (conative-v1 + coercion-v2): turns the anecdotal "gpt-5.4-mini diverges across instruments" into a per-model × per-construction disagreement statistic |NLI gap − FC gap|. **Near-null finding — instrument fragility is NOT pervasive:** large disagreement (50 pp) is confined to the single gpt-5.4-mini × conative cell; the other 8 cells are ≤ 20.8 pp (coercion-v2 cells ≤ 10 pp). Advances [`open-question/instrument-sensitivity-constructional-inference`](findings/open-questions/instrument-sensitivity-constructional-inference.md); anchored (indirect) to [`resource/scivetti-2025-cxnli-dataset`](base/resources/scivetti-2025-cxnli-dataset.md).

- [`findings/results/argument-structure-coercion-v2.md`](findings/results/argument-structure-coercion-v2.md) — status: proposed (2026-05-29); **the project's first *off-ceiling* probe** — a conflicting-cue stress test of the two add-direction Tier-4 positives (caused-motion + way). Built to separate H-deep (computes the inference, would withhold it under a resolving cue) from H-default (fires a "this-frame→yes" template). **Result: the v1 ceilings are cue-sensitive, not a brittle template** — with an explicit clause denying the added inference, all three models drop to **floor (cue affirm 0–20%, 60–100 pp drop from canonical), 3/3 models, both instruments, both constructions** (template reading 0/3). Construction asymmetry: caused-motion declines cognition-verb coercions; the way-construction coerces traversal even on self-motion-precluding verbs (carries traversal independent of the verb) but is still cancelled by the cue. **Calibration: explicit cue only** (subtler world-knowledge cue = v2b); internal-contrast-only; `contingent-on: []` (promoted 2026-05-31); pre/post-run adversarial passes were orchestrator self-reviews (subagent 529 outage). Refines the v1 add-direction results. Cost $0.093. (0 NA / 360 calls.)
- [`findings/results/aann-behavioral-gradient-v2.md`](findings/results/aann-behavioral-gradient-v2.md) — status: proposed (2026-06-12); **the AANN probe finally ran — SUPPORTED on the pre-registered map.** Under the freshly-ratified behavioral instrument, all 3 models' prompted graded acceptability **rank-tracks the human Mahowald Exp-2 MTurk gradient** (cell-level Spearman 0.70 / 0.68 / 0.75 over 204 adjective×noun-class cells, CIs excluding 0; Zipf frequency guard and noun-class-marginal guard both clean) **and replicates the class gradient on frequency-matched held-out adjectives** (0.83 / 0.81 / 0.75; uneven by noun class — temporal stratum negative, caveat 2). Tier-0 manipulation check 23–24/24. Read through the instrument's bounds: gradient-*tracking*, not meaning-*representation*; the conjecture's inferential half untested (natural v3). Verification chain: pre-run critic (added the noun-class guard that a zero-adjective-information responder would otherwise have passed), frozen PREREG, independent post-run verifier (0 mismatches). Anchored to [`resource/mahowald-2023-aann-stimuli`](base/resources/mahowald-2023-aann-stimuli.md); `contingent-on: []`. Cost $0.3125 (billed; 1,782 calls, 0 missing).
- [`findings/results/way-construction-traversal-v1.md`](findings/results/way-construction-traversal-v1.md) — status: proposed (2026-05-29); **the project's own way-construction minimal-pair probe** (the third own-design argument-structure probe; does the construction *add* a self-motion / path-traversal entailment onto non-motion verbs — *whistled his way down the hall*?). **Confirmed above the ratified bar**: affirm-path-traversal rate 77.8–100%, gap (way − location control) 77.7–100 pp, 3/3 models, both instruments; the anti-motion verb-reading guard holds at/near ceiling; the idiomatic over-generalization guard is at 0% and the ctrl-motion positive floor at 100%. gpt-5.4-mini is the conservative outlier (declines 4–5 scattered items *hum/eat/chat/snack* as "may or may not have moved" — a cautious entailment bar, not verb-reading failure; it affirms the anti-motion items at 100%). Patterns with caused-motion (the "add" direction is easy). Lead caveat: ceiling on relatively easy controls. Anchored to [`resource/scivetti-2025-cxnli-dataset`](base/resources/scivetti-2025-cxnli-dataset.md); `contingent-on: []`. Cost $0.072. (0 NA / 360 calls.)
- [`findings/results/comparative-correlative-covariation-v1.md`](findings/results/comparative-correlative-covariation-v1.md) — status: proposed (2026-05-29); **the project's first probe of its own design to run** (charter §5.4). The 2026 decoder panel deploys the comparative correlative's covariation meaning at ceiling — construction-driven (T1 +80–90pp over matched controls), direction-tracking (T2 inverse-flip 95–100%), n-gram-robust (T3 no atypical collapse) — matching the Scivetti ≈0.90 human baseline (93–100%). - [`findings/results/scivetti-let-alone-working-surface-v1.md`](findings/results/scivetti-let-alone-working-surface-v1.md) — status: proposed (2026-06-20); **the let-alone failure is largely an OUTPUT-CHANNEL artifact** — the witness-seeking control [`essay/output-channel-confound`](findings/essays/output-channel-confound.md) prescribes. Re-ran the SAME 24 let-alone + 30 comparative-correlative (ceiling control) items under a **working surface** (step-by-step + `FINAL:` tag), format-only, gemini reasoning-effort held constant. **2/3 LIFT to the human ≈0.90 baseline on the same items** (claude 0.542→0.792, gemini 0.667→0.917; within-item sign test 7/1, p=0.035; control PRESERVED) → the session-57 scalar-phrasal dissociation was substantially a forced-single-token channel effect masking *scalar/serial* inference, **not** a content-type competence boundary. gpt-5.4-mini did **not** recover (0.375) but largely **declined** the surface (16/24 bare, 0 reasoning tokens) → channel **non-uptake**, not channel-controlled. Fires `output-channel-confound` trigger (a) + refines its scope (the cut is "is the inference serial," not "is it NLI"); trigger (b) stays open (needs uptake-inducing arm). **Refines** [`result/scivetti-cxnli-answer-key-v1`](findings/results/scivetti-cxnli-answer-key-v1.md). Anchored to [`resource/scivetti-2025-cxnli-dataset`](base/resources/scivetti-2025-cxnli-dataset.md); `contingent-on: []`. Cost $0.3164. (0 NA / 162 calls; independent pre-run critic GO + post-run verifier REPRODUCED.)
- [`findings/results/scivetti-let-alone-forced-decomposition-v1.md`](findings/results/scivetti-let-alone-forced-decomposition-v1.md) — status: proposed (2026-06-20); **forcing the weakest model to actually USE the working surface partly closes its let-alone gap but does not reach the human baseline** — the uptake-inducing arm session 58 named. Re-ran the SAME 24 let-alone + 30 comparative-correlative items with a **forced** 3-step decomposition (mandatory, construction-neutral, answer-blind; no demo items), single-variable vs session 58's *offered* surface. **Uptake INDUCED for all 3** (gpt's median let-alone completion 8→120 tokens, 24/24 worked, closing session 58's "channel-not-taken-up" gap). With the channel genuinely exercised, gpt rose 0.375→**0.583** (+0.21, 7/2, **but sign-test p=0.090 → UNCHANGED**, underpowered) and **stays BELOW** the ≈0.90 baseline where claude (0.833) / gemini (0.875) sit → a **partial** output-channel effect (part channel-bounded, part survives the exercised channel), the closest in-repo **trigger-(b) candidate**, not a clean firing. claude/gemini stay at baseline + control PRESERVED (scaffold benign). **Refines** [`result/scivetti-let-alone-working-surface-v1`](findings/results/scivetti-let-alone-working-surface-v1.md); supports [`essay/output-channel-confound`](findings/essays/output-channel-confound.md). Anchored to [`resource/scivetti-2025-cxnli-dataset`](base/resources/scivetti-2025-cxnli-dataset.md); `contingent-on: []`. Cost $0.3921. - [`findings/results/scivetti-let-alone-repeated-runs-v1.md`](findings/results/scivetti-let-alone-repeated-runs-v1.md) — status: proposed (2026-06-21, session 64); **five repeated temp-0 runs PIN the let-alone jitter — it is ceiling-protected and model-specific, and gpt's below-baseline residual is robust to it.** The trigger-(g) / [`essay/point-estimate-is-a-draw`](findings/essays/point-estimate-is-a-draw.md) trigger-(a) repeated-run measurement: the **byte-identical** forced-decomposition instrument scored **K=5** times at temp 0 over the **same frozen 63 items** (all shas == s62). **Trigger (a) FIRES (all three models):** the comp-corr ceiling control **did not jitter** (range 0.000 claude/gemini; 0.033 gpt) while near-chance let-alone swung (**gpt range 0.121**, claude 0.061, gemini 0.030) → jitter is **near-chance-concentrated, ceiling-protected, model-specific** (the ~±0.12 is *gpt's* number; trigger (b) un-fired). **gpt residual robust:** every one of 5 runs **< 0.90** (band [0.545, 0.667]); de-noised majority-vote **0.606** [0.437, 0.753] → session 62's CONFIRMS-RESIDUAL was **not** a low draw (trigger (d) case). **Refines s62:** "gemini deterministic" → "**most stable**" (2/33 churn); claude's s62 0.708 was a low draw (within-session test band [0.750, 0.792]); same-session spread a **lower bound** (claude's cross-session s60→s62 swing 0.125 > within-session test range 0.042). **Refines** [`result/scivetti-let-alone-powered-rerun-v1`](findings/results/scivetti-let-alone-powered-rerun-v1.md); supports [`essay/point-estimate-is-a-draw`](findings/essays/point-estimate-is-a-draw.md) + [`essay/output-channel-confound`](findings/essays/output-channel-confound.md). Anchored to [`resource/scivetti-2025-cxnli-dataset`](base/resources/scivetti-2025-cxnli-dataset.md); `contingent-on: []`. Stayed inside the ratified v1/v2 relational operationalization; `anchor: internal-contrast-only`; `contingent-on: []`. ### Open questions

- [`findings/open-questions/relational-meaning-pilot.md`](findings/open-questions/relational-meaning-pilot.md) — what minimal two-agent setup constitutes evidence that meaning is being constituted *between* agents rather than computed inside each? **The pilot was built and run** (GO = Tom's Decision 9, [`decisions/resolved/relational-pilot-go`](decisions/resolved/relational-pilot-go.md)) → [`result/relational-reference-game-v1`](findings/results/relational-reference-game-v1.md) (first-class null, 2026-05-31; yardstick ratified 2026-06-12) and the sharper [`result/relational-history-perturbation-v2`](findings/results/relational-history-perturbation-v2.md) (inconclusive, 2026-06-12). **Stays open**: the bottom rung of the second ladder is still unclimbed; remaining arms = artifact-resolved perturbation follow-up, image referents, cross-family dyads.
- [`findings/open-questions/constructional-vs-frequency-confound.md`](findings/open-questions/constructional-vs-frequency-confound.md) — status: open (2026-05-29); how to separate constructional-meaning sensitivity from an n-gram/frequency confound in surprisal-contrast probes (form-level).
- [`findings/open-questions/distributional-vs-inferential-constructional.md`](findings/open-questions/distributional-vs-inferential-constructional.md) — status: open (2026-05-29); granting constructional sensitivity, what minimal evidence shows it is inferential-role tracking vs. a distributional shadow (meaning-level; downstream of the frequency question).
- [`findings/open-questions/lexical-polysemy-gradience.md`](findings/open-questions/lexical-polysemy-gradience.md) — status: **open — largely addressed** (updated 2026-05-31; Tom kept it open); the project's first **lexical** (non-grammatical) wedge: does LLM in-context sense behavior reproduce the graded polysemy lexicographers document, or collapse to discrete senses — separable from a context-similarity (`distributional`) shadow? **Largely answered by the lexical line** ([`result/lexical-sense-gradience-v1`](findings/results/lexical-sense-gradience-v1.md) + [`result/lexical-polysemy-homonymy-v2`](findings/results/lexical-polysemy-homonymy-v2.md) + [`result/lexical-polysemy-homonymy-v3`](findings/results/lexical-polysemy-homonymy-v3.md)): graded-sense tracking IS present and beats the context-similarity shadow (clauses a+c); the distinctive *discrete-regime* sub-arm (clause b) is **not established** — a powered null on homonymy-enriched WiC (not falsified). Anchors WiC / WordNet / DWUG now all in-repo.
- [`findings/open-questions/lexical-bridging-context-gradience.md`](findings/open-questions/lexical-bridging-context-gradience.md) — status: **answered** (2026-06-22); re-opened the dormant lexical axis on the conjecture's one untested clause (Prediction 4): do **bridging** (sense-ambiguous) contexts elicit **intermediate, lower-confidence** same/different behavior — *within-item* uncertainty, distinct from v1's *cross-item* monotonic correlation? Surfaced the two gates (operationalization of "less-confident"; a human anchor for "genuinely bridging"); **both RATIFIED 2026-06-21 (session 75, cross-session)** → [`decisions/resolved/lexical-bridging-context-operationalization`](decisions/resolved/lexical-bridging-context-operationalization.md) (B+C fixed panel, per-axis reading) and [`decisions/resolved/lexical-bridging-context-anchor`](decisions/resolved/lexical-bridging-context-anchor.md) (DWUG stratum + WiC poles, ≥3-rater floor, claim **capped to usage-similarity**). **The probe RAN (session 77)** → [`result/lexical-bridging-context-v1`](findings/results/lexical-bridging-context-v1.md): a **clean null, 3/3 — graded SCALE, ungraded COMMITMENT** (intermediate position on bridging items, but clear-item confidence + ≈0 decline + near-zero dispersion); within-item discreteness complementary to v3's between-stratum null.
- [`findings/open-questions/relational-arrival-order-beyond-text.md`](findings/open-questions/relational-arrival-order-beyond-text.md) — status: open (2026-06-22); revives the dormant relational order-composition axis. Rungs (i)/(ii) are occupied (thin/single-reader-recoverable); rung (iii)'s *rich* side (an arrival-order surplus not recoverable from a final content+timestamp record) is **documented structurally closed for text-only stimuli** (a transcript IS such a record — the [`essay/transcript-ceiling`](findings/essays/transcript-ceiling.md) argument). The live question: does that surplus exist in any **non-text** medium? Names candidate media with the honest default that the closure is plausibly **medium-general**; sketches one candidate probe (anchor flagged `pending`). A **non-spend planning artifact** — opens no probe, freezes no operationalization, ratifies nothing.
- [`findings/open-questions/gradience-population-not-moment.md`](findings/open-questions/gradience-population-not-moment.md) — status: open (2026-06-22); a **cross-level** synthesis question raised by the lexical bridging null. The same shape recurs at three semantic levels — graded/structured in the **aggregate**, discrete/uncommitted in the **moment**: lexical (graded scale, ungraded commitment — [`result/lexical-bridging-context-v1`](findings/results/lexical-bridging-context-v1.md)), relational ([`essay/aggregation-not-constitution`](findings/essays/aggregation-not-constitution.md)), constructional ([`essay/preference-without-commitment`](findings/essays/preference-without-commitment.md)). Is this a **general constraint on distributional competence** or three level-specific facts that merely rhyme? Names the disanalogies (different instruments/anchor-status per leg; one human-anchored leg, two `internal-contrast-only`) and the discriminating evidence (a shared-instrument cross-level probe; an output-channel working-surface re-run). **The named output-channel re-run has now run (session 79)** → [`result/lexical-bridging-context-working-surface-v1`](findings/results/lexical-bridging-context-working-surface-v1.md): the lexical "discrete-moment" leg comes out **largely channel-controlled (firmer, not dissolved)**, with two caveats (claude's confidence self-report softens; gpt declined the surface). Distinct from [`essay/graded-scale-ungraded-commitment`](findings/essays/graded-scale-ungraded-commitment.md) (the lexical home), which it cites. A **non-spend** question page. **Matured 2026-06-22 (session 80)** into the forward bet [`conjecture/cross-level-gradience-aggregate-not-moment`](findings/conjectures/cross-level-gradience-aggregate-not-moment.md) + its operationalization gate [`decisions/resolved/cross-level-shared-instrument-operationalization`](decisions/resolved/cross-level-shared-instrument-operationalization.md) (ratified session 82, ADOPT DEFAULT), and generalized into the method essay [`essay/cross-level-convergence-ladder`](findings/essays/cross-level-convergence-ladder.md). **The shared-instrument discriminator has now RUN (session 84) → DISSOLUTION (3/3 models)** → [`result/cross-level-shared-instrument-v1`](findings/results/cross-level-shared-instrument-v1.md): the deflationary default is now evidenced, not merely assumed.
- [`findings/open-questions/instrument-sensitivity-constructional-inference.md`](findings/open-questions/instrument-sensitivity-constructional-inference.md) — status: open (updated 2026-05-31); does measured constructional-inference competence depend on the **elicitation instrument** (NLI vs forced-choice)? Motivated by own-design results where gpt-5.4-mini diverges across instruments. **Now characterized by three results** ([`result/comparative-correlative-covariation-v3`](findings/results/comparative-correlative-covariation-v3.md), [`result/caused-motion-near-miss-v2c`](findings/results/caused-motion-near-miss-v2c.md), [`result/instrument-disagreement-reanalysis-v1`](findings/results/instrument-disagreement-reanalysis-v1.md)): **two sources** of fragility — a model-specific one (gpt-5.4-mini's excluded-middle slip under negation) and a *general* NLI-vs-FC pragmatics/entailment effect (all 3 models) — and the re-analysis bounds its pervasiveness (large disagreement confined to gpt × conative). Stays **open** (no dedicated cross-instrument design run). Gives a typed home to the theory page's "instrument-fragility as a first-class variable"; conditions how every Tier-4 result is read.
- [`findings/open-questions/constructional-divergence-probe.md`](findings/open-questions/constructional-divergence-probe.md) — status: **answered** (2026-05-29) → [`result/cxnli-distinction-divergence-v1`](findings/results/cxnli-distinction-divergence-v1.md). The minimal project-run probe it called for was built and run (panel-as-subjects on Scivetti base vs. distinction); the divergence gap reproduced. Its named follow-up — the project's *own* minimal-pair conative probe with a memorization/frequency arm — was **also built and run this session** → [`result/conative-minimal-pair-divergence-v1`](findings/results/conative-minimal-pair-divergence-v1.md) (which *refines* the distinction collapse: clean minimal pairs show more conative competence than the adversarial distinction items).

## How to extend this file

When you add a typed page, add a one-line entry here in the right section. When you retire one, leave the line and append `— retired YYYY-MM-DD`. Do not delete entries; the audit trail matters.
